152: 39: 
153: 40: ## 🔭 Overview
154: 41: 
155: 42: **UHC** is a full-featured, production-ready Flutter application designed for university health centers. It provides a seamless experience for **students** and **staff** to book medical appointments, a dedicated **doctor dashboard** for managing appointments and schedules with QR-verified check-ins, and powerful **admin tools** for managing doctors, departments, and analytics — all backed by Firebase's real-time infrastructure.
156: 43: 
157: 44: ### ✨ Why UHC?
158: 45: 
159: 46: | | |
160: 47: |---|---|
161: 48: | 🌐 **Multilingual** | Full RTL support with English, Arabic, and Kurdish translations |
162: 49: | ⚡ **Performant** | Scalability-audited for large users, bounded Firestore queries, parallel fetching, and composite indexes |
163: 50: | 🔒 **Secure** | Role-based access control with server-side Cloud Functions for privileged operations |
164: 51: | 🎨 **Modern UI** | Material Design 3, smooth animations, dark mode, and responsive layouts |
165: 52: | 📱 **Cross-Platform** | Single codebase for Android, iOS, and Web |
166: 53: 
167: 54: ---
168: 55: 
169: 56: ## 🚀 Key Features
170: 57: 
171: 58: <details>
172: 59: <summary><b>👤 Patient Portal</b></summary>
173: 60: 
174: 61: - **Smart Authentication** — Email/password, Google Sign-In, and password recovery
175: 62: - **Appointment Booking** — Browse by department or doctor, pick available time slots, and confirm instantly
176: 63: - **Appointment Management** — View upcoming/past appointments, reschedule, or cancel with reason tracking
177: 64: - **Medical Documents** — Upload and organize lab results, prescriptions, and imaging reports
178: 65: - **Push Notifications** — Appointment reminders and in-app notification center
179: 66: - **Profile Management** — Edit personal info, change password, upload profile photo
180: 67: - **QR Code** — Generate QR codes for appointments
181: 68: - **Dark Mode** — System-aware or manual theme toggle
182: 69: 
183: 70: </details>
184: 71: 
185: 72: <details>
186: 73: <summary><b>👨‍⚕️ Doctor Dashboard</b></summary>
187: 74: 
188: 75: - **Dashboard Overview** — Personalized greeting, daily stats (patients, appointments, completed, pending), and quick access to upcoming appointments
189: 76: - **Appointment Management** — View upcoming and past appointments with staggered card animations, patient avatars, and status badges
190: 77: - **QR-Verified Check-In** — Time-gated confirm button (5 min before → 10 min after appointment); opens camera QR scanner to verify patient presence; manual fallback after 5 failed scans
191: 78: - **Schedule Management** — Interactive calendar with day/week/month views, color-coded time slots (booked, available, past, blocked)
192: 79: - **Appointment Details** — Full appointment view with patient info, medical notes editor, and action buttons (confirm, complete, cancel, no-show)
193: 80: - **Patient Profiles** — View patient details, profile photos, medical info, and appointment history from within appointment context
194: 81: - **Doctor Profile & Settings** — Edit specialization, bio, qualifications; configure notifications, language, and theme
195: 82: - **Push Notifications** — Real-time alerts for new bookings, cancellations, and status changes
196: 83: - **Consistent Design Language** — Matches patient/staff UI with shared widgets, staggered animations, skeleton loaders, and theme-aware styling
197: 84: 
198: 85: </details>
199: 86: 
200: 87: <details>
201: 88: <summary><b>🔧 Admin Console</b></summary>
202: 89: 
203: 90: - **Real-Time Dashboard** — Live KPIs: total users, doctors, appointments, and revenue
204: 91: - **Department Management** — Create departments with custom color, icon (155+ options), and per-day working hours
205: 92: - **Doctor Management** — Full CRUD with schedule constraints tied to department hours
206: 93: - **User Management** — View all users, assign roles, toggle account status
207: 94: - **Analytics** — Interactive charts for appointment trends and department performance
208: 95: - **Reports** — Export CSV reports for appointments, doctors, users, and revenue
209: 96: </details>
210: 97: 
211: 98: <details>
212: 99: <summary><b>🏥 Supported Departments</b></summary>
213: 100: 
214: 101: | Department | Department |
215: 102: |:---|:---|
216: 103: | General Medicine | Orthopedics |
217: 104: | Pediatrics | Laboratory |
218: 105: | Dermatology | Radiology |
219: 106: | Psychiatry | Cardiology |
220: 107: | Rehabilitation | Pharmacy |
221: 108: 
222: 109: > Departments are fully configurable via the admin console — add new ones with custom icons, colors, and working hours.
223: 110: 
224: 111: </details>
225: 112:

227: 114: 
228: 115: ## 🏗 Architecture & Tech Stack
229: 116: 
230: 117: ### Technology Overview
231: 118: 
232: 119: | Layer | Technology | Purpose |
233: 120: |:---|:---|:---|
234: 121: | **Framework** | Flutter 3.x / Dart 3.5+ | Cross-platform UI toolkit |
235: 122: | **State Management** | Provider | Reactive state with ChangeNotifier |
236: 123: | **Authentication** | Firebase Auth, Google Sign-In | Secure multi-method authentication |
237: 124: | **Database** | Cloud Firestore | Real-time NoSQL document database |
238: 125: | **File Storage** | Firebase Storage | Medical document & image hosting |
239: 126: | **Messaging** | Firebase Cloud Messaging | Push notifications |
240: 127: | **Server Logic** | Firebase Cloud Functions (TypeScript) | Privileged admin operations |
241: 128: | **Local Storage** | SharedPreferences | User preferences & theme persistence |
242: 129: | **Notifications** | flutter_local_notifications | Scheduled local reminders |
243: 130: | **UI Framework** | Material Design 3, Google Fonts | Modern design language |
244: 131: | **Animations** | Lottie, flutter_animate | Smooth onboarding & micro-interactions |
245: 132: | **Charts** | fl_chart | Admin analytics & dashboards |
246: 133: | **Calendar** | table_calendar | Date selection for appointments |
247: 134: | **QR Codes** | qr_flutter, mobile_scanner | Patient QR generation & doctor-side scanning |
248: 135: | **Localization** | ARB files, flutter_localizations | EN / AR / KU with RTL support |
249: 136: 
250: 137: ### Application Architecture
251: 138: 
252: 139: ```
253: 140: ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
254: 141: │                    Presentation Layer                   │
255: 142: │         Screens  ·  Widgets  ·  Animations              │
256: 143: ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
257: 144: │                   State Management                      │
258: 145: │                     Provider                            │
259: 146: ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
260: 147: │                     Data Layer                          │
261: 148: │            Models  ·  Repositories                      │
262: 149: ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
263: 150: │                   Services Layer                        │
264: 151: │       FCM  ·  Local Notifications  ·  Utilities         │
265: 152: ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
266: 153: │                   Firebase Backend                      │
267: 154: │  Auth  ·  Firestore  ·  Storage  ·  Functions  ·  FCM   │
268: 155: └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
269: 156: ```

273: 160: ## 📁 Project Structure
274: 161: 
275: 162: ```
276: 163: uhc/

278: 165: │   ├── core/

280: 167: │   │   ├── localization/           # Kurdish material localizations
281: 168: │   │   ├── theme/                  # Material 3 theme configuration

283: 170: │   │   └── widgets/                # Shared widgets (buttons, text fields, cards, skeletons)
284: 171: │   ├── data/
285: 172: │   │   ├── models/                 # User, Doctor, Appointment, Department, Notification models
286: 173: │   │   └── repositories/           # Firestore data access layer
287: 174: │   ├── l10n/

295: 182: │   │   ├── splash/                 # Animated splash screen

302: 189: │   │   │   ├── main_shell.dart     # Bottom navigation shell
303: 190: │   │   │   ├── home/               # Home feed

305: 192: │   │   │   ├── booking/            # Appointment booking flow
306: 193: │   │   │   ├── browse_doctors/     # Doctor list & schedule viewer
307: 194: │   │   │   ├── departments/        # Department browsing & filtering
308: 195: │   │   │   ├── documents/          # Medical document upload & viewer
309: 196: │   │   │   ├── profile/            # Profile & edit profile
310: 197: │   │   │   └── location/           # Health center map & directions
311: 198: │   │   ├── doctor/                 # Doctor dashboard (separate shell)
312: 199: │   │   │   ├── doctor_shell.dart   # 5-tab bottom navigation shell
313: 200: │   │   │   ├── dashboard/          # Overview, stats, today's appointments

315: 202: │   │   │   ├── schedule/           # Calendar-based schedule management
316: 203: │   │   │   ├── profile/            # Doctor profile & edit profile
317: 204: │   │   │   └── qr/                 # QR code scanner for appointment check-in
318: 205: │   │   └── admin/                  # Admin management console
319: 206: │   │       ├── dashboard/          # Admin KPI dashboard
320: 207: │   │       ├── departments/        # Department CRUD with form dialog
321: 208: │   │       ├── doctors/            # Doctor CRUD with schedule dialog
322: 209: │   │       ├── users/              # User management with form dialog
323: 210: │   │       ├── analytics/          # Appointment analytics & charts
324: 211: │   │       └── reports/            # CSV report generation & export
325: 212: │   ├── services/                   # Auth, FCM, local notifications, Cloud Function wrappers
326: 213: │   └── utils/                      # Helper functions
327: 214: ├── functions/                      # Firebase Cloud Functions (TypeScript)
328: 215: ├── assets/
329: 216: │   ├── images/                     # Static images
330: 217: │   ├── animations/                 # Lottie animation files
331: 218: │   └── icons/                      # Custom icon assets
332: 219: ├── android/                        # Android platform configuration
333: 220: ├── ios/                            # iOS platform configuration
334: 221: ├── web/                            # Web platform configuration
335: 222: ├── docs/                           # Internal documentation & audit reports
336: 223: ├── firestore.rules                 # Firestore security rules (role-based)
337: 224: ├── firestore.indexes.json          # Composite index definitions for optimized queries
338: 225: └── pubspec.yaml                    # Dependencies & metadata
339: 226: ```

343: 230: ## 🚀 Getting Started
344: 231: 
345: 232: ### Prerequisites
346: 233: 
347: 234: | Requirement | Version |
348: 235: |:---|:---|
349: 236: | Flutter SDK | 3.x or later |
350: 237: | Dart SDK | 3.5+ |
351: 238: | Node.js | 18+ *(for Cloud Functions)* |
352: 239: | Firebase CLI | Latest |
353: 240: | Android Studio / Xcode | For platform builds |
354: 241: 
355: 242: ### Quick Start
356: 243: 
357: 244: ```bash
358: 245: # 1. Clone the repository
359: 246: git clone <repository-url>
360: 247: cd uhc
361: 248: 
362: 249: # 2. Install Flutter dependencies
363: 250: flutter pub get
364: 251: 
365: 252: # 3. Configure Firebase (see next section)
366: 253: 
367: 254: # 4. Generate localization files
368: 255: flutter gen-l10n
369: 256: 
370: 257: # 5. Run the app
371: 258: flutter run
372: 259: ```
373: 260: 
374: 261: ### Cloud Functions Setup
375: 262: 
376: 263: ```bash
377: 264: # Navigate to functions directory
378: 265: cd functions
379: 266: 
380: 267: # Install Node.js dependencies
381: 268: npm install
382: 269: 
383: 270: # Deploy functions to Firebase
384: 271: firebase deploy --only functions
385: 272: ```
386: 273: 
387: 274: ---
388: 275: 
389: 276: ## 🔥 Firebase Configuration
390: 277: 
391: 278: ### Required Services
392: 279: 
393: 280: Enable the following in your [Firebase Console](https://console.firebase.google.com):
394: 281: 
395: 282: - ✅ **Authentication** — Enable Email/Password and Google Sign-In providers
396: 283: - ✅ **Cloud Firestore** — Create database in production mode
397: 284: - ✅ **Firebase Storage** — Enable for file uploads
398: 285: - ✅ **Cloud Messaging** — Enable for push notifications
399: 286: - ✅ **Cloud Functions** — Upgrade project to Blaze plan (required for Node.js functions)
400: 287: 
401: 288: ### Platform Configuration
402: 289: 
403: 290: | Platform | Config File | Location | Instructions |
404: 291: |:---|:---|:---|:---|
405: 292: | Android | `google-services.json` | `android/app/` | Download from Firebase Console |
406: 293: | iOS | `GoogleService-Info.plist` | `ios/Runner/` | Download from Firebase Console |
407: 294: | Web | Firebase config object | `web/index.html` | Copy config from Firebase Console |
408: 295: 
409: 296: ### Android Configuration
410: 297: 
411: 298: Ensure your `android/app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml` includes these permissions:
412: 299: 
413: 300: ```xml
414: 301: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.CAMERA"/>
415: 302: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.RECEIVE_BOOT_COMPLETED"/>
416: 303: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.VIBRATE" />
417: 304: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.POST_NOTIFICATIONS"/>
418: 305: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.SCHEDULE_EXACT_ALARM" android:maxSdkVersion="32"/>
419: 306: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.USE_EXACT_ALARM"/>
420: 307: <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.WAKE_LOCK"/>
421: 308: ```
422: 309: 
423: 310: ### iOS Configuration
424: 311: 
425: 312: Add these keys to `ios/Runner/Info.plist` for permissions:
426: 313: 
427: 314: ```xml
428: 315: <!-- Camera & Photo Library for Profile/Document Uploads -->
429: 316: <key>NSCameraUsageDescription</key>
430: 317: <string>We need access to your camera to take profile photos and scan medical documents.</string>
431: 318: <key>NSPhotoLibraryUsageDescription</key>
432: 319: <string>We need access to your photo library to upload profile photos and medical records.</string>
433: 320: 
434: 321: <!-- Notifications -->
435: 322: <key>UIBackgroundModes</key>
436: 323: <array>
437: 324:     <string>fetch</string>
438: 325:     <string>remote-notification</string>
439: 326: </array>
440: 327: ```
441: 328: 
442: 329: ### Firestore Collections
443: 330: 
444: 331: | Collection | Description |
445: 332: |:---|:---|
446: 333: | `users` | User profiles, roles, and preferences |
447: 334: | `doctors` | Doctor profiles, specializations, and schedules |
448: 335: | `departments` | Department metadata — name, icon, color, working hours |
449: 336: | `appointments` | Booking records with status tracking, QR check-in, and scan failure counts |
450: 337: | `notifications` | Per-user notification history |
451: 338: | `user_tokens` | FCM device tokens per user (used by Cloud Functions for push delivery) |
452: 339: | `medical_documents` | Uploaded file metadata and storage references |
453: 340: 
454: 341: ---
455: 342: 
456: 343: ## ⚙️ Cloud Functions
457: 344: 
458: 345: Server-side functions handle privileged operations that require Firebase Admin SDK access:
459: 346: 
460: 347: | Function | Description | Access |
461: 348: |:---|:---|:---|
462: 349: | `createDoctorAccount` | Creates a doctor account in Auth + Firestore with the `doctor` role | 🔒 Admin |
463: 350: | `updateDoctorEmail` | Updates a doctor's email in both Auth and Firestore | 🔒 Admin |
464: 351: | `deleteDoctorAccount` | Removes a doctor from Auth and Firestore completely | 🔒 Admin |
465: 352: | `resetDoctorPassword` | Resets a doctor's password without requiring the old one | 🔒 Admin |
466: 353: | `createUserAccount` | Creates a user account in Auth + Firestore with a specified role | 🔒 Admin |
467: 354: | `onNotificationCreated` | Firestore trigger — sends FCM push when a notification document is created | 🔄 Auto |
468: 355: | `sendTopicNotification` | Sends broadcast push notifications to FCM topics (e.g. announcements) | 🔒 Admin |
469: 356: 
470: 357: > **Security Note:** These functions enforce admin-only access to prevent unauthorized privilege escalation. All critical account mutations are handled server-side.
471: 358: 
472: 359: ---
473: 360: 
474: 361: ## 🔐 User Roles & Permissions
475: 362: 
476: 363: | Role | Capabilities |
477: 364: |:---|:---|
478: 365: | **Student** | Book/manage appointments, upload documents, view own records |
479: 366: | **Staff** | Same as Student — campus staff access |
480: 367: | **Doctor** | View assigned appointments, manage schedule and availability |
481: 368: | **Admin** | Full system access — manage users, doctors, departments, view analytics, export reports |
482: 369: 
483: 370: > **Note:** The first admin user must be created manually in Firestore.
484: 371: > 
485: 372: > **How to create an Admin:**
486: 373: > 1. Sign up as a regular user in the app.
487: 374: > 2. Go to Firebase Console > Firestore Database > `users` collection.
488: 375: > 3. Find your user document.
489: 376: > 4. Change the `role` field from `"student"` to `"admin"`.
490: 377: > 5. Restart the app to see the Admin Dashboard.
491: 378: 
492: 379: ---
493: 380: 
494: 381: ## 📦 Building for Production
495: 382: 
496: 383: ```bash
497: 384: # ── Android ──────────────────────────
498: 385: flutter build apk --release          # APK
499: 386: flutter build appbundle --release     # AAB (Play Store)
500: 387: 
501: 388: # ── iOS ──────────────────────────────
502: 389: flutter build ios --release
503: 390: 
504: 391: # ── Web ──────────────────────────────
505: 392: flutter build web --release
506: 393: ```

523: 410: 
524: 411: ## 📝 Changelog
525: 412: 
526: 413: <details open>
527: 414: <summary><b>v1.10.0</b> — April 2026</summary>
528: 415: 
529: 416: #### ⚡ Scalability & Performance Audit (20k–50k Concurrent Users)
530: 417: A comprehensive code audit identified and resolved 13 scalability issues to ensure the app performs smoothly at scale (20,000–50,000 concurrent users).
531: 418: 
532: 419: ##### 🔴 Critical Fixes
533: 420: - **Bounded Firestore Queries** — Added `.limit()` to every unbounded query across the entire codebase. Previously, methods like `getUpcomingAppointments()`, `getPastAppointments()`, and `getAllDoctorAppointments()` would download entire document collections (potentially 500k+ docs at scale). All queries now have appropriate limits (500–1000 docs per method).
534: 421: - **N+1 Query Elimination** — Replaced sequential `for`-loop photo fetching with `Future.wait()` for parallel execution. Loading 10 doctor photos now takes ~200ms instead of ~3,000ms (one network round-trip vs. ten sequential ones).
535: 422: - **Admin User Stream Limit** — Added `.limit(200)` with **"Load More" pagination** to the admin User Management screen. Starts with 200 users, each tap loads 200 more — the admin can browse all users without loading 50k at once.
536: 423: - **Notification Query Optimization** — Replaced `getUnreadCount()` (which downloaded all unread documents) with Firestore's `.count()` aggregation — zero document downloads, server-side counting.
537: 424: 
538: 425: ##### 🟡 Moderate Fixes
539: 426: - **8 Composite Firestore Indexes** — Defined composite indexes for the most common query patterns (`doctorId + appointmentDate`, `patientId + appointmentDate`, `userId + createdAt`, `userId + isRead`, etc.) to enable efficient server-side filtering instead of client-side in-memory filtering.
540: 427: - **Batch Operation Chunking** — All batch write operations (`markAllAsRead`, `deleteAllNotifications`, `deleteAllUserAppointments`, `deleteFutureDailySummaries`) now chunk into groups of 500 to respect Firestore's batch limit. Previously, batches with >500 operations would fail silently.
541: 428: - **Booking Screen Query Limit** — Added `.limit(500)` to the booking screen's appointment fetch, preventing download of a doctor's entire appointment history on every calendar date tap.
542: 429: - **Doctor Search Caching** — `searchDoctors()` now caches the doctor list in memory and filters locally, instead of re-fetching the entire `doctors` collection on every keystroke.
543: 430: - **Analytics & Reports Pagination** — Reports and analytics now use **cursor-based auto-pagination** (fetching in 5,000-doc batches using `startAfterDocument`) instead of hard limits. The admin clicks "Generate" and gets a **complete** CSV export or accurate stats, regardless of how many documents exist. Each individual Firestore request stays bounded at 5,000 docs to stay safe.
544: 431: 
545: 432: ##### 🟢 Minor Fixes
546: 433: - **FCM Token Refresh Leak** — Fixed duplicate `onTokenRefresh` listeners by cancelling previous subscriptions before re-registering.
547: 434: - **Notification Tap Listener Leak** — Fixed `onMessageTapped` listeners being registered multiple times upon re-initialization, causing duplicate navigation.
548: 435: - **Server-Side Daily Summary Filtering** — `deleteFutureDailySummaries()` now uses a `where('type', isEqualTo: 'dailySummary')` server-side filter instead of downloading all user notifications.
549: 436: 
550: 437: ##### 📊 Projected Impact
551: 438: 
552: 439: | Metric | Before | After |
553: 440: |:---|:---|:---|
554: 441: | Firestore reads (50k users/day) | ~40,000,000+ | ~5,000,000 |
555: 442: | Estimated monthly cost (50k users) | $150–250+ | $15–25 |
556: 443: | Doctor appointment load time (2k+ appointments) | 3–8 seconds | <500ms |
557: 444: | Doctor photo fetching (10 unique doctors) | ~3,000ms sequential | ~200ms parallel |
558: 445: 
559: 446: #### 📁 Files Changed
560: 447: 
561: 448: | File | Key Changes |
562: 449: |:---|:---|
563: 450: | `lib/data/repositories/appointment_repository.dart` | `.limit()` on all 5 query methods, chunked batch deletes |
564: 451: | `lib/data/repositories/notification_repository.dart` | `count()` aggregation, stream limits, chunked batches, server-side filtering |
565: 452: | `lib/providers/appointment_provider.dart` | Parallel doctor photo fetching via `Future.wait()` |
566: 453: | `lib/providers/doctor_appointment_provider.dart` | Parallel patient photo fetching via `Future.wait()` |
567: 454: | `lib/providers/doctor_provider.dart` | In-memory caching for doctor search |
568: 455: | `lib/providers/notification_provider.dart` | Fixed FCM listener memory leak (`_messageTapSubscription`) |
569: 456: | `lib/screens/admin/users/user_management_screen.dart` | "Load More" pagination (200 per page) |
570: 457: | `lib/screens/patient/booking/booking_screen.dart` | `.limit(500)` on booked slots query |
571: 458: | `lib/screens/admin/analytics/appointment_analytics_screen.dart` | Cursor-based auto-pagination (5k batches) |
572: 459: | `lib/screens/admin/reports/reports_screen.dart` | `_paginatedFetch()` helper, auto-pagination on all 3 report generators |
573: 460: | `lib/services/fcm_service.dart` | Fixed duplicate token refresh listeners |
574: 461: | `firestore.indexes.json` | Added 8 composite indexes |
575: 462: 
576: 463: </details>
577: 464: 
578: 465: <details>
579: 466: <summary><b>v1.9.0</b> — March 2026</summary>
580: 467: 
581: 468: #### ⏱ Auto No-Show System
582: 469: - **Automated Status Updates** — Pending appointments that have passed their scheduled time by 60 minutes (30-minute slot + 30-minute grace period) are automatically marked as "No Show" when the doctor opens their dashboard.
583: 470: - **System Attribution** — Auto no-show updates are tagged with `statusUpdatedBy: 'system_auto'` to distinguish them from manual doctor actions.
584: 471: 
585: 472: #### 📷 Profile Image Size Limits
586: 473: - **25 MB Upload Limit** — All profile image uploads (patient, doctor, and admin) now enforce a 25 MB file size limit with a clear error message, preventing excessive storage consumption.
587: 474: 
588: 475: #### 🔐 Google Authentication Hardening
589: 476: - **Account-Only Sign-In** — Google Sign-In now only allows existing, admin-created accounts to log in. Signing in with a Google account that isn't already registered is blocked, preventing unauthorized account creation.
590: 477: - **Profile Photo Preservation** — Signing in with a linked Google account no longer overwrites the user's custom profile image with the generic Google avatar.
591: 478: 
592: 479: #### 📅 Doctor Appointment Display Fix
593: 480: - **Today's Appointments Visible** — Fixed a date comparison bug where today's appointments were not showing in the doctor's "Upcoming" tab. Corrected the start-of-day boundary logic to include the current date.
594: 481: 
595: 482: #### 📁 Document Screen Fixes
596: 483: - **Stream Caching** — Fixed Firestore stream recreation during document uploads that caused performance issues and UI churn. The stream is now cached in widget state and only recreated when the user ID changes.
597: 484: - **Mounted Check** — Added `mounted` guard before accessing context after async dialog operations to prevent "context used after dispose" errors.
598: 485: 
599: 486: #### 📁 Files Changed
600: 487: 
601: 488: | File | Key Changes |
602: 489: |:---|:---|
603: 490: | `lib/providers/doctor_appointment_provider.dart` | Auto no-show logic with 60-minute cutoff |
604: 491: | `lib/screens/patient/profile/edit_profile_screen.dart` | 25 MB image upload limit |
605: 492: | `lib/screens/doctor/profile/edit_doctor_profile_screen.dart` | 25 MB image upload limit |
606: 493: | `lib/providers/auth_provider.dart` | Google sign-in restricted to existing accounts, photo preservation |
607: 494: | `lib/screens/doctor/appointments/doctor_appointments_screen.dart` | Fixed today's appointment date boundary |
608: 495: | `lib/screens/patient/documents/medical_documents_screen.dart` | Stream caching, mounted check |
609: 496: | `lib/screens/doctor/documents/doctor_patient_documents_screen.dart` | Stream caching, mounted check |
610: 497: 
611: 498: </details>
612: 499: 
613: 500: <details>
614: 501: <summary><b>v1.8.0</b> — March 2026</summary>
615: 502: 
616: 503: #### 🔔 FCM Push Notification Infrastructure (BUGs 6–10)
617: 504: - **Server-Side FCM Sending** — Added `onNotificationCreated` Cloud Function: a Firestore `onDocumentCreated` trigger that automatically sends FCM push notifications when a notification document is created. Looks up user FCM tokens from the `user_tokens` collection and sends via `admin.messaging().send()` with Android high-priority channel and iOS alert/badge/sound support. Automatically cleans up stale tokens on `invalid-registration-token` errors.
618: 505: - **Topic Broadcast Function** — Added `sendTopicNotification` callable Cloud Function for admins to send push notifications to FCM topics (e.g. `announcements`, `department_*`).
619: 506: - **Patient FCM Token Registration** — Fixed `main_shell.dart` to call `notificationProvider.initialize(userId)` instead of `loadNotifications()`, ensuring patient devices register their FCM token, subscribe to topics, and start notification listeners.
620: 507: - **FCMService Singleton** — Refactored `FCMService` into a proper singleton with a factory constructor and `_initialized` guard, preventing duplicate notification handlers across `main.dart` and `NotificationProvider`.
621: 508: - **Platform Detection** — Replaced hardcoded `'android'` platform string with dynamic `Platform.isIOS ? 'ios' : 'android'` detection in both initial token save and `onTokenRefresh` listener.
622: 509: - **Logout FCM Cleanup** — `AuthProvider.signOut()` now calls `FCMService.removeTokenFromDatabase()` and `unsubscribeUserFromTopics()` before Firebase Auth sign-out, preventing stale token accumulation.
623: 510: 
624: 511: #### 🔔 Notification System Consolidation
625: 512: - **Unified Notification Settings** — Removed individual push/email notification toggles from patient `ProfileScreen` and doctor `DoctorProfileScreen`. All notification preferences are now managed exclusively through the shared `NotificationSettingsScreen`.
626: 513: - **Real-Time Notification Streams** — `NotificationProvider` now uses Firestore real-time streams (`streamNotifications`, `streamUnreadCount`) instead of one-time fetches, so the UI auto-updates when new notifications arrive.
627: 514: - **Doctor Daily Summary Settings** — Consolidated daily summary toggle and time picker into `NotificationSettingsScreen`, visible only to doctors. Time selection uses `SharedPreferences` and syncs to the scheduling system.
628: 515: - **Dead Code Removal** — Removed unused `showAppointmentConfirmed()` and `showAppointmentCancelled()` methods from `LocalNotificationService`.
629: 516: 
630: 517: #### ⏰ Appointment Reminder Timing Fix
631: 518: - **Exact Appointment Time** — Reminders now use `exactAppointmentTime` (date + timeSlot combined) instead of `appointmentDate` (midnight), so 1-week, 24-hour, and 1-hour reminders fire relative to the actual appointment time, not midnight.
632: 519: - **Reschedule Reminders** — Rescheduled appointments correctly rebuild the exact DateTime from the new date and time slot.
633: 520: 
634: 521: #### 📬 Doctor Status Notifications to Patients
635: 522: - **Confirmation Notification** — When a doctor confirms an appointment, the patient now receives a Firestore notification with the doctor's name, date, and time slot.
636: 523: - **No-Show Notification** — When a doctor marks a patient as no-show, the patient receives a notification and old reminders are cleaned up.
637: 524: - **Completion Notification** — When an appointment is completed, the patient receives a thank-you notification and old reminders are deleted.
638: 525: 
639: 526: #### 📷 Doctor Profile Photo Editing
640: 527: - **Large Avatar Editor** — Doctor edit profile screen now features a 120px tappable photo circle (matching patient profile style) with camera icon overlay and "Tap to change photo" text.
641: 528: - **Image Picker** — Camera, gallery, and remove options via bottom sheet with themed icons.
642: 529: - **Firebase Storage Upload** — Photo is uploaded on save and the URL is synced to both `doctors` and `users` Firestore collections.
643: 530: - **Read-Only Card Cleanup** — Removed duplicate small avatar from the read-only card, replaced with an info icon to avoid visual clutter.
644: 531: 
645: 532: #### 🎨 UI Improvements
646: 533: - **Appointment Detail Layout** — Fixed text overflow in the doctor appointment detail info rows by switching to `Expanded` flex layout instead of `Spacer` + `Flexible`.
647: 534: - **Patient Detail FittedBox** — Patient info values now scale down gracefully using `FittedBox` instead of being truncated with `TextOverflow.ellipsis`.
648: 535: - **Home Screen Book Button** — "Book Appointment Now" text is now wrapped in `Flexible` with `maxLines: 1` to prevent overflow on narrow screens or long translations.
649: 536: 
650: 537: #### 📁 Files Changed
651: 538:

653: 540: |:---|:---|
654: 541: | `functions/src/index.ts` | Added `onNotificationCreated` and `sendTopicNotification` Cloud Functions |
655: 542: | `lib/services/fcm_service.dart` | Singleton pattern, idempotent init, platform detection |
656: 543: | `lib/providers/auth_provider.dart` | FCM cleanup on sign-out |

821: 708: Contributions are welcome! Please follow these steps:
822: 709: 
823: 710: 1. **Fork** the repository
824: 711: 2. **Create** your feature branch
825: 712:    ```bash
826: 713:    git checkout -b feature/amazing-feature
827: 714:    ```
828: 715: 3. **Commit** your changes with a descriptive message
829: 716:    ```bash
830: 717:    git commit -m "feat: add amazing feature"
831: 718:    ```
832: 719: 4. **Push** to your branch
833: 720:    ```bash
834: 721:    git push origin feature/amazing-feature
835: 722:    ```
836: 723: 5. **Open** a Pull Request
837: 724: 
838: 725: > Please ensure your code follows the project's lint rules (`flutter analyze`) and includes appropriate tests.

<system-reminder>
Instructions from: C:\Develop\Project App\UHC\uhc\docs\AGENTS.md
# AGENTS.md — UHC (University Health Center)

## Project Overview

Flutter/Dart healthcare appointment booking app with Firebase backend.
Dart SDK ^3.5.0, Provider (ChangeNotifier) state management, Firestore + Auth + Cloud Functions (TypeScript/Node.js 22).
Localization: English, Arabic, Kurdish via ARB files. No code generation (no freezed/json_serializable).

## Build / Run / Test

```bash
flutter pub get                          # Install dependencies
flutter gen-l10n                         # Generate l10n (MUST run before analyze/build)
flutter analyze                          # Static analysis
flutter test                             # Run all tests
flutter test test/widget_test.dart       # Run single test file
flutter test --name "test name here"     # Run single test by name
dart format .                            # Format code
dart format --set-exit-if-changed .      # Format check (CI)
flutter run                              # Debug run
flutter build apk --release              # Release APK

# Cloud Functions (from functions/ directory)
npm install && npm run build             # Install + compile TS
npm run serve                            # Local emulator
```

**CI** (`.github/workflows/dart.yml`): `pub get` -> `gen-l10n` -> `analyze` -> `test` on push/PR to `main`.

## Project Structure

```
lib/
  main.dart                 # Entry point, 7 ChangeNotifierProviders, AppNavigator state machine
  firebase_options.dart     # Auto-generated — NEVER edit
  core/
    constants/              # AppColors, AppStrings, AppAssets (private constructor utility classes)
    theme/                  # AppTheme — Material 3 light/dark (Poppins headings, Roboto body)
    utils/                  # Locale utilities, dynamic content translation maps
    widgets/                # PrimaryButton, CustomTextField, GlassmorphicCard, skeletons
  data/
    models/                 # 5 models: User, Appointment, Doctor, Department, Notification
    repositories/           # Firestore CRUD — one per collection
  providers/                # 7 ChangeNotifiers: auth, theme, locale, appointment, notification, doctor, doctor_appointment
  services/                 # Firebase SDK wrappers (AuthService, FCMService, etc.)
  screens/                  # Screens grouped by feature (auth/, home/, booking/, doctor/, admin/)
  l10n/                     # ARB files (app_en.arb, app_ar.arb, app_ku.arb) + generated
functions/src/index.ts      # 5 admin-only callable Cloud Functions (Gen2)
firestore.rules             # Security rules with role-based access
```

## Code Style

### Formatting
- `dart format` default settings. **Trailing commas** everywhere. **Single quotes** only.

### Imports (3 groups, no blank lines between)
1. `dart:` core libraries
2. `package:` dependencies
3. Relative project imports (`'../services/...'`) — never `package:uhc/...`

### Naming

| Element            | Convention                            | Example                              |
|--------------------|---------------------------------------|--------------------------------------|
| Files              | `snake_case`                          | `auth_provider.dart`                 |
| Classes            | `PascalCase`                          | `AuthProvider`, `AppointmentModel`   |
| Enums              | `PascalCase` name, `camelCase` values | `enum UserRole { student, doctor }`  |
| Variables/fields   | `camelCase`, explicit types preferred | `final String id;`                   |
| Private members    | `_` prefix                            | `_authService`, `_handleError()`     |
| Constants          | `static const camelCase`              | `static const Color primary = ...`   |
| Widget builders    | `_build` prefix                       | `_buildHeader()`                     |
| Constants classes  | Private constructor                   | `class AppColors { AppColors._(); }` |

### Types
- Explicit type annotations on fields and method signatures. `final` without type OK for obvious locals.
- Always annotate return types. Nullable: `String?`, fallbacks with `??`.
- `const` constructors on StatelessWidgets. `const` children wherever possible.

## Key Patterns

### Screen Lifecycle
- `StatefulWidget`. Load data in `initState` via `addPostFrameCallback`.
- **Always check `mounted`** before `setState` after any `await`.
- **Always dispose** controllers/subscriptions. `super.dispose()` last.
- Dark mode: `final isDark = Theme.of(context).brightness == Brightness.dark;`
- Break large `build()` into `_buildXxx()` methods.

### Navigation
- No router package. `AppNavigator` state machine: splash -> onboarding -> auth -> role shell.
- `UserRole.doctor` -> `DoctorShell`, others -> `MainShell`. Both use `IndexedStack`.
- Screens receive navigation callbacks (`VoidCallback?`) — no direct `Navigator.push` from children.

### Provider Pattern
```dart
class XxxProvider extends ChangeNotifier {
  bool _isLoading = false;
  String? _error;
  // public getters, no public setters

  Future<bool> doAction() async {
    _isLoading = true; _error = null; notifyListeners();
    try {
      // await service call
      return true;
    } catch (e) {
      _error = e.toString(); return false;
    } finally {
      _isLoading = false; notifyListeners();
    }
  }
}
```
Providers are independent — no cross-provider injection.

### Data Models
All `final` fields. `factory fromFirestore(DocumentSnapshot)` with `??` fallbacks, `toFirestore()`, `copyWith(...)`. Enums at top of file.

### Firestore Repositories
- Single-field `.where()` + in-memory filtering (avoids composite indexes).
- Create: `.add()` then `.update({'id': docRef.id})`.
- Error: `catch (e) { debugPrint(...); return []; }`.

### Error Handling

| Layer        | Pattern                                                          |
|--------------|------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Services     | Catch `FirebaseAuthException`, map to user strings, rethrow      |
| Providers    | `catch (e)` -> set `_error` -> `notifyListeners()` -> return `false` |
| Repositories | `catch (e)` -> `debugPrint(...)` -> return `[]` or `null`        |
| Screens      | Check `isLoading`/`error` inline, show `SnackBar` on failure     |

### Localization
- Strings in ARB files (`lib/l10n/`). Access: `AppLocalizations.of(context)!.key`.
- Run `flutter gen-l10n` after any ARB change.

### Cloud Functions (TypeScript)
- Admin-only: verify `context.auth` + Firestore role check.
- Gen2 `onCall`, typed `CallableRequest<T>`, throw `HttpsError`.
- Strict TS: `noImplicitReturns`, `noUnusedLocals`, `strict`.

## Never Edit Manually

- `lib/firebase_options.dart` — generated by FlutterFire CLI
- `lib/l10n/app_localizations*.dart` — generated by `flutter gen-l10n`

</system-reminder>
```

28: 2. Routing currently has only one special shell: doctor. All non-doctor users use `MainShell` (`lib/main.dart`).

31: 5. Firestore rules currently allow owner write on full `users/{userId}` document, which is a privilege-escalation risk for `role` and other sensitive fields (`firestore.rules`).

43:   - `superAdmin`: can manage admins and perform all admin operations
44:   - `admin`: operational management only, no admin-governance edits
45:

47:

49:   - `primary`

53:   - exactly one `primary`
54:   - exactly one `backup`
55:   - no API path that leaves system in invalid state
56:

60:   - `users.view`, `users.manageNonAdmin`

62:   - `departments.view`, `departments.manage`
63:   - `analytics.view`
64:   - `reports.view`, `reports.export`
65:   - `notifications.send`
66: - Super Admin bypasses admin permission checks (full access).
67: - Admin UI becomes permission-driven (what can be seen and changed).
68: 
69: ### 4) Trust boundary
70: 
71: - Sensitive operations must be callable functions only.
72: - Client-side direct writes for sensitive fields/actions are removed.
73: - Firestore rules block privilege mutation by normal client updates.

122:    - `assignSuperAdminSlot(targetUid, slotType)` where `slotType in {primary, backup}`
123:      - MUST run inside Firestore `runTransaction(...)` (no plain `set()`/`update()` path)
124:      - transaction reads current super-admin documents + slot occupancy, validates constraints, then writes atomically
125:      - prevents race conditions where concurrent requests could create duplicate `primary` or duplicate `backup`

267: 3. `users`: `role + superAdminType`
268: 4. `admin_audit_logs`: `createdAt`
269: 5. `admin_audit_logs`: `actorUid + createdAt`
270: 6. `admin_audit_logs`: `targetUid + createdAt`
271: 7. `admin_audit_logs`: `action + createdAt`
272: 
273: ---
274: 
275: ## Phase 8 - Bootstrap and migration runbook
276: 
277: 1. Manual bootstrap first Super Admin:
278:    - set `role: superAdmin`
279:    - set `superAdminType: primary`
280: 2. Deploy backend functions + rules
281: 3. App deploy with Super Admin shell
282: 4. Use Super Admin UI to create/assign backup slot
283: 5. Keep existing admins as admins
284: 6. Assign admin permissions progressively
285: 
286: ---
287: 
288: ## Test Plan
289: 
290: ### A) Security tests (must pass)
291: 
292: 1. Student/staff/doctor cannot self-promote to admin/superAdmin
293: 2. Admin cannot edit admin role/status/password/delete
294: 3. Only Super Admin can run governance functions
295: 4. Super Admin slot constraints always enforced (primary + backup only)
296: 
297: ### B) Functional tests
298: 
299: 1. Super Admin can perform every required admin-governance action
300: 2. Admin has view-only admin section
301: 3. Permission toggles immediately affect screen/action visibility
302: 4. Audit logs are created for all governance actions
303: 
304: ### C) UX tests
305: 
306: 1. New screens match existing app style tokens/components
307: 2. Web and mobile responsive behavior verified
308: 3. Existing doctor/patient/admin flows remain stable
309: 
310: ---
311: 
312: ## Delivery Sequence (recommended)
313: 
314: 1. Backend guards + governance functions + audit logs
315: 2. Firestore rules hardening
316: 3. Model/routing updates
317: 4. Super Admin shell + core screens
318: 5. Existing admin screen migration to functions + RBAC
319: 6. Indexes + QA + rollout
320: 
321: ---
322: 
323: ## Acceptance Criteria
324: 
325: 1. `superAdmin` role exists end-to-end (model, routing, backend, rules).
326: 2. Exactly two Super Admin slots are enforced (`primary`, `backup`).
327: 3. Super Admin can fully govern admin accounts.
328: 4. Admin users can view admin accounts but cannot modify them.
329: 5. Sensitive admin operations are callable-function based (not direct client writes).
330: 6. All admin-governance actions are auditable.
331: 7. UI remains visually consistent with current UHC style on web and mobile.

176:   bool hasPermission(String permissionKey) {
177:     if (isSuperAdmin) return true;
178:     if (!isAdmin) return false;
179:     // If no permissions object yet (legacy admin), grant full access
180:     if (adminPermissions == null) return true;
181:     return adminPermissions!.getByKey(permissionKey);

1: /// Granular admin permissions for RBAC
2: ///
3: /// Super Admin bypasses all permission checks (full access).
4: /// Admin users have a permissions map that controls what they can see and do.
5: class AdminPermissions {
6:   // User management
7:   final bool usersView;
8:   final bool usersManageNonAdmin;
9: 
10:   // Doctor management
11:   final bool doctorsView;

20:

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 129.7s)

**Phase 0 Review**
- I reviewed Phase 0 against `docs/plans/Plan_Super_Admin_RBAC.md` and your checklist; verdict is **Changes required** (1 blocker).
- Verified good: `UserRole.superAdmin` added, `UserModel` extended (`isSuperAdmin`, `superAdminType`, `adminPermissions`), `displayRole` updated, `toFirestore`/`copyWith` updated, `AdminPermissions` model created, `AdminAuditLog` model created.
- Quality checks passed: `flutter analyze` (no issues) and `flutter test` (all passed).

- **Blocker:** reachable crash when editing a super admin user.
- In `lib/screens/admin/users/user_form_dialog.dart:632`, dropdown `initialValue` can be `UserRole.superAdmin`.
- In `lib/screens/admin/users/user_form_dialog.dart:642`, dropdown items exclude `UserRole.superAdmin`.
- Super admins are still listed in `lib/screens/admin/users/user_management_screen.dart:141` (only doctors excluded) and have edit action at `lib/screens/admin/users/user_management_screen.dart:319`, so this path is real.

- **Security warning (non-blocking for Phase 0, but important):** direct role/status writes still exist at `lib/screens/admin/users/user_management_screen.dart:690` and `lib/screens/admin/users/user_management_screen.dart:724`; do not bootstrap real super admins before Phase 1 + Phase 2 are in place.

1. Recommended fix for Antigravity now: make super admin rows view-only in user management (hide edit/toggle/role actions for `superAdmin`) to remove the crash path and reduce risk.
2. Alternative fix: allow `superAdmin` in dropdown only when it is the current value, and disable changing it from this dialog.

Once that blocker is fixed, send Phase 0 again and I’ll re-review immediately.

index 8dcea48..a1562b1 100644
--- a/functions/src/index.ts
+++ b/functions/src/index.ts
@@ -6,6 +6,86 @@ admin.initializeApp();
 const db = admin.firestore();
 const auth = admin.auth();
 
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Shared Guards & Helpers
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/** Throws if caller is not authenticated. Returns the uid. */
+function requireAuth(context: { auth?: { uid: string } }): string {
+    if (!context.auth) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
+            'unauthenticated',
+            'You must be logged in to perform this action.'
+        );
+    }
+    return context.auth.uid;
+}
+
+/** Fetches the caller's user document. Throws if not found. */
+async function getCallerUserDoc(uid: string): Promise<FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot> {
+    const doc = await db.collection('users').doc(uid).get();
+    if (!doc.exists) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Caller user document not found.');
+    }
+    return doc;
+}
+
+/** Returns true if user role is admin or superAdmin. */
+function isAdminOrSuperAdmin(role: string | undefined): boolean {
+    return role === 'admin' || role === 'superAdmin';
+}
+
+/** Throws if caller is not admin or superAdmin. */
+function requireAdminOrSuperAdmin(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot): void {
+    const role = callerDoc.data()?.role;
+    if (!isAdminOrSuperAdmin(role)) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only admins can perform this action.');
+    }
+}
+
+/** Throws if caller is not superAdmin. */
+function requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot): void {
+    if (callerDoc.data()?.role !== 'superAdmin') {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only Super Admins can perform this action.');
+    }
+}
+
+/** Throws if caller (admin) lacks the given permission. SuperAdmin bypasses. */
+function requirePermission(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot, permissionKey: string): void {
+    const data = callerDoc.data();
+    if (!data) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Caller data missing.');
+    if (data.role === 'superAdmin') return; // bypass
+    if (data.role !== 'admin') {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only admins can perform this action.');
+    }
+    const perms = data.adminPermissions as Record<string, boolean> | undefined;
+    // Legacy admins without permissions object get full access
+    if (!perms) return;
+    if (!perms[permissionKey]) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', `Missing permission: ${permissionKey}`);
+    }
+}
+
+/** Writes an entry to admin_audit_logs collection. */
+async function writeAdminAuditLog(params: {
+    actorUid: string;
+    actorRole: string;
+    actorName?: string;
+    targetUid: string;
+    targetName?: string;
+    targetRoleBefore?: string;
+    targetRoleAfter?: string;
+    action: string;
+    before?: Record<string, unknown>;
+    after?: Record<string, unknown>;
+    metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
+}): Promise<void> {
+    await db.collection('admin_audit_logs').add({
+        ...params,
+        createdAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+    });
+}
+

 );
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Super Admin Governance Functions
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/**
+ * Create an admin account. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const createAdminAccount = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        email: string; password: string; fullName: string;
+        phoneNumber?: string; dateOfBirth?: string; photoUrl?: string;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const data = request.data;
+
+        if (!data.email || !data.password || !data.fullName) {
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Missing required fields.');
+        }
+        if (data.password.length < 6) {
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Password must be at least 6 characters.');
+        }
+
+        try {
+            const userRecord = await auth.createUser({
+                email: data.email, password: data.password,
+                displayName: data.fullName, emailVerified: false,
+            });
+            const now = admin.firestore.Timestamp.now();
+            await db.collection('users').doc(userRecord.uid).set({
+                email: data.email, fullName: data.fullName, role: 'admin',
+                phoneNumber: data.phoneNumber || null, photoUrl: data.photoUrl || null,
+                dateOfBirth: data.dateOfBirth ? admin.firestore.Timestamp.fromDate(new Date(data.dateOfBirth)) : null,
+                isActive: true, adminPermissions: null, // full access by default
+                notificationSettings: { email: true, push: true, sms: false },
+                language: 'en', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
+                bloodType: null, allergies: null, studentId: null, staffId: null,
+            });
+            await writeAdminAuditLog({
+                actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: callerDoc.data()!.role,
+                actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+                targetUid: userRecord.uid, targetName: data.fullName,
+                targetRoleAfter: 'admin', action: 'admin.create',
+            });
+            return { success: true, userId: userRecord.uid, message: 'Admin account created successfully' };
+        } catch (error: unknown) {
+            if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'code' in error) {
+                const e = error as { code: string };
+                if (e.code === 'auth/email-already-exists')
+                    throw new functions.https.HttpsError('already-exists', 'A user with this email already exists.');
+            }
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('internal', 'Failed to create admin account.');
+        }
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Change an admin user's role. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const changeAdminRole = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; newRole: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, newRole } = request.data;
+
+        if (!targetUid || !newRole) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Missing targetUid or newRole.');
+        if (!['admin', 'student', 'staff'].includes(newRole))
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Invalid role. Cannot assign doctor or superAdmin via this function.');
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        const targetData = targetDoc.data()!;
+        const oldRole = targetData.role;
+
+        if (oldRole === 'superAdmin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot change a Super Admin role via this function.');
+
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({ role: newRole, updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now() });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetData.fullName,
+            targetRoleBefore: oldRole, targetRoleAfter: newRole,
+            action: oldRole === 'admin' ? 'admin.demote' : 'admin.promote',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: `Role changed from ${oldRole} to ${newRole}` };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Activate or deactivate an admin. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const setAdminActiveStatus = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; isActive: boolean }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, isActive } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        if (targetDoc.data()!.role === 'superAdmin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot deactivate a Super Admin via this function.');
+
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({ isActive, updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now() });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: isActive ? 'admin.activate' : 'admin.deactivate',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: isActive ? 'Admin activated' : 'Admin deactivated' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Reset an admin's password. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const resetAdminPassword = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; newPassword: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, newPassword } = request.data;
+
+        if (!newPassword || newPassword.length < 6)
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Password must be at least 6 characters.');
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+
+        await auth.updateUser(targetUid, { password: newPassword });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: 'admin.passwordReset',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'Password reset successfully' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Delete an admin account. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const deleteAdminAccount = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        const targetData = targetDoc.data()!;
+        if (targetData.role === 'superAdmin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot delete a Super Admin account.');
+
+        try { await auth.deleteUser(targetUid); } catch (e) { console.log('Auth user may not exist:', e); }
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).delete();
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetData.fullName,
+            targetRoleBefore: targetData.role, action: 'admin.delete',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'Admin account deleted successfully' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Force sign-out a user by revoking refresh tokens. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const forceSignOutUser = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+
+        await auth.revokeRefreshTokens(targetUid);
+        // Also remove FCM token to stop push notifications
+        await db.collection('user_tokens').doc(targetUid).delete().catch(() => {});
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: 'admin.forceSignOut',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'User sessions revoked' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Set admin permissions. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const setAdminPermissions = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        targetUid: string;
+        permissions: Record<string, boolean>;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, permissions } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        if (targetDoc.data()!.role !== 'admin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Permissions can only be set on admin accounts.');
+
+        const oldPerms = targetDoc.data()!.adminPermissions || {};
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({
+            adminPermissions: permissions,
+            updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+        });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: 'admin.permissionsUpdate',
+            before: oldPerms as Record<string, unknown>,
+            after: permissions as Record<string, unknown>,
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'Permissions updated' };
+    }
+);
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Super Admin Slot Management (strict two-account model)
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/**
+ * Assign a user to a Super Admin slot (primary or backup).
+ * Runs inside a Firestore transaction to enforce constraints:
+ * - Max 2 superAdmins total
+ * - Exactly one primary, exactly one backup
+ * Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const assignSuperAdminSlot = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        targetUid: string; slotType: 'primary' | 'backup';
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, slotType } = request.data;
+
+        if (!['primary', 'backup'].includes(slotType))
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'slotType must be primary or backup.');
+
+        const result = await db.runTransaction(async (tx) => {
+            // Read current super admins
+            const superAdminsSnap = await tx.get(
+                db.collection('users').where('role', '==', 'superAdmin')
+            );
+            const currentSlots = superAdminsSnap.docs.map(d => ({
+                uid: d.id, slotType: d.data().superAdminType as string,
+            }));
+
+            // Check if this slot is already occupied by someone else
+            const existingSlotHolder = currentSlots.find(s => s.slotType === slotType);
+            if (existingSlotHolder && existingSlotHolder.uid !== targetUid) {
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
+                    'failed-precondition',
+                    `The ${slotType} slot is already occupied. Use rotateSuperAdminSlot to replace.`
+                );
+            }
+
+            // Check max 2
+            const otherSuperAdmins = currentSlots.filter(s => s.uid !== targetUid);
+            if (otherSuperAdmins.length >= 2) {
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Maximum 2 Super Admin slots reached.');
+            }
+
+            // Read target
+            const targetRef = db.collection('users').doc(targetUid);
+            const targetSnap = await tx.get(targetRef);
+            if (!targetSnap.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+            const oldRole = targetSnap.data()!.role;
+
+            tx.update(targetRef, {
+                role: 'superAdmin', superAdminType: slotType,
+                updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+            });
+            return { oldRole, targetName: targetSnap.data()!.fullName };
+        });
+
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: result.targetName,
+            targetRoleBefore: result.oldRole, targetRoleAfter: 'superAdmin',
+            action: 'superAdmin.slotAssign',
+            after: { slotType } as Record<string, unknown>,
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: `Assigned ${slotType} Super Admin slot` };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Rotate a Super Admin slot: demote the current holder and promote the replacement.
+ * Runs inside a transaction to ensure atomicity.
+ * Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const rotateSuperAdminSlot = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        slotType: 'primary' | 'backup'; replacementUid: string;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { slotType, replacementUid } = request.data;
+
+        if (!['primary', 'backup'].includes(slotType))
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'slotType must be primary or backup.');
+
+        const result = await db.runTransaction(async (tx) => {
+            // Find current holder of this slot
+            const slotSnap = await tx.get(
+                db.collection('users')
+                    .where('role', '==', 'superAdmin')
+                    .where('superAdminType', '==', slotType)
+            );
+            if (slotSnap.empty) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', `No current ${slotType} Super Admin found.`);
+
+            const currentHolder = slotSnap.docs[0];
+            const currentHolderUid = currentHolder.id;
+
+            if (currentHolderUid === replacementUid)
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Replacement is already the slot holder.');
+
+            // Read replacement
+            const replacementRef = db.collection('users').doc(replacementUid);
+            const replacementSnap = await tx.get(replacementRef);
+            if (!replacementSnap.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Replacement user not found.');
+
+            // Demote current holder to admin
+            tx.update(db.collection('users').doc(currentHolderUid), {
+                role: 'admin', superAdminType: admin.firestore.FieldValue.delete(),
+                updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+            });
+            // Promote replacement
+            tx.update(replacementRef, {
+                role: 'superAdmin', superAdminType: slotType,
+                updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+            });
+            return {
+                demotedName: currentHolder.data().fullName,
+                demotedUid: currentHolderUid,
+                promotedName: replacementSnap.data()!.fullName,
+                promotedOldRole: replacementSnap.data()!.role,
+            };
+        });
+
+        // Log both actions
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid: result.demotedUid, targetName: result.demotedName,
+            targetRoleBefore: 'superAdmin', targetRoleAfter: 'admin',
+            action: 'superAdmin.slotRotate', metadata: { slotType, direction: 'demote' },
+        });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid: replacementUid, targetName: result.promotedName,
+            targetRoleBefore: result.promotedOldRole, targetRoleAfter: 'superAdmin',
+            action: 'superAdmin.slotRotate', metadata: { slotType, direction: 'promote' },
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: `Rotated ${slotType} Super Admin slot` };
+    }
+);

```

15:     if (!context.auth) {
16:         throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
17:             'unauthenticated',
18:             'You must be logged in to perform this action.'
19:         );
20:     }

25: async function getCallerUserDoc(uid: string): Promise<FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot> {
26:     const doc = await db.collection('users').doc(uid).get();
27:     if (!doc.exists) {
28:         throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Caller user document not found.');
29:     }
30:     return doc;

34: function isAdminOrSuperAdmin(role: string | undefined): boolean {
35:     return role === 'admin' || role === 'superAdmin';
36: }
37: 
38: /** Throws if caller is not admin or superAdmin. */
39: function requireAdminOrSuperAdmin(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot): void {
40:     const role = callerDoc.data()?.role;
41:     if (!isAdminOrSuperAdmin(role)) {
42:         throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only admins can perform this action.');
43:     }
44: }

47: function requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot): void {
48:     if (callerDoc.data()?.role !== 'superAdmin') {
49:         throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only Super Admins can perform this action.');
50:     }
51: }
52: 
53: /** Throws if caller (admin) lacks the given permission. SuperAdmin bypasses. */
54: function requirePermission(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot, permissionKey: string): void {
55:     const data = callerDoc.data();
56:     if (!data) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Caller data missing.');
57:     if (data.role === 'superAdmin') return; // bypass
58:     if (data.role !== 'admin') {
59:         throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only admins can perform this action.');
60:     }
61:     const perms = data.adminPermissions as Record<string, boolean> | undefined;
62:     // Legacy admins without permissions object get full access
63:     if (!perms) return;
64:     if (!perms[permissionKey]) {
65:         throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', `Missing permission: ${permissionKey}`);
66:     }
67: }
