405:         try {
406:             // Get doctor document to find userId
407:             const doctorDoc = await db.collection('doctors').doc(data.doctorId).get();
408:             if (!doctorDoc.exists) {
409:                 throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Doctor not found.');
410:             }
411: 
412:             const doctorData = doctorDoc.data();
413:             const userId = doctorData?.userId;
414: 
415:             if (!userId || userId.startsWith('sample_')) {
416:                 throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
417:                     'failed-precondition',
418:                     'This doctor does not have an associated auth account.'
419:                 );
420:             }
421: 
422:             // Update password
423:             await auth.updateUser(userId, { password: data.newPassword });
424: 
425:             return { success: true, message: 'Password reset successfully' };
426:         } catch (error) {
427:             console.error('Error resetting doctor password:', error);
428:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
429:                 'internal',
430:                 'Failed to reset doctor password.'
431:             );
432:         }
433:     }
434: );
435: 
436: interface CreateUserData {
437:     email: string;
438:     password: string;
439:     fullName: string;
440:     role: 'admin' | 'student' | 'staff';
441:     phoneNumber?: string;
442:     dateOfBirth?: string; // ISO date string
443:     studentId?: string;
444:     staffId?: string;
445:     photoUrl?: string;
446: }
447: 
448: /**
449:  * Cloud Function to create a user account (admin, student, or staff)
450:  * This creates both the Firebase Auth user and the Firestore user document
451:  */
452: export const createUserAccount = functions.https.onCall(
453:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<CreateUserData>) => {
454:         const data = request.data;
455:         const context = request;
456: 
457:         // Check if the caller is authenticated and is an admin
458:         if (!context.auth) {
459:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
460:                 'unauthenticated',
461:                 'You must be logged in to perform this action.'
462:             );
463:         }
464: 
465:         // Verify caller is admin
466:         const callerDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(context.auth.uid).get();
467:         if (!callerDoc.exists || !isAdminOrSuperAdmin(callerDoc.data()?.role)) {
468:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
469:                 'permission-denied',
470:                 'Only admins can create user accounts.'
471:             );
472:         }
473: 
474:         // Validate required fields
475:         if (!data.email || !data.password || !data.fullName || !data.role) {
476:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
477:                 'invalid-argument',
478:                 'Missing required fields: email, password, fullName, role'
479:             );
480:         }
481: 
482:         // Validate role (prevent creating doctors through this function)
483:         if (!['admin', 'student', 'staff'].includes(data.role)) {
484:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
485:                 'invalid-argument',
486:                 'Invalid role. Must be admin, student, or staff.'
487:             );
488:         }
489: 
490:         // Validate password strength
491:         if (data.password.length < 6) {
492:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
493:                 'invalid-argument',
494:                 'Password must be at least 6 characters long'
495:             );
496:         }
497: 
498:         try {
499:             // Create Firebase Auth user
500:             const userRecord = await auth.createUser({
501:                 email: data.email,
502:                 password: data.password,
503:                 displayName: data.fullName,
504:                 emailVerified: false,
505:             });
506: 
507:             const now = admin.firestore.Timestamp.now();
508: 
509:             // Create user document
510:             await db.collection('users').doc(userRecord.uid).set({
511:                 email: data.email,
512:                 fullName: data.fullName,
513:                 role: data.role,
514:                 phoneNumber: data.phoneNumber || null,
515:                 photoUrl: data.photoUrl || null,
516:                 dateOfBirth: data.dateOfBirth ? admin.firestore.Timestamp.fromDate(new Date(data.dateOfBirth)) : null,
517:                 studentId: data.studentId || null,
518:                 staffId: data.staffId || null,
519:                 isActive: true,
520:                 notificationSettings: {
521:                     email: true,
522:                     push: true,
523:                     sms: false,
524:                 },
525:                 language: 'en',
526:                 createdAt: now,
527:                 updatedAt: now,
528:             });
529: 
530:             return {
531:                 success: true,
532:                 userId: userRecord.uid,
533:                 message: `${data.role.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + data.role.slice(1)} account created successfully`,
534:             };
535:         } catch (error: unknown) {
536:             console.error('Error creating user account:', error);
537: 
538:             // Handle specific Firebase Auth errors
539:             if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'code' in error) {
540:                 const firebaseError = error as { code: string; message?: string };
541:                 if (firebaseError.code === 'auth/email-already-exists') {
542:                     throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
543:                         'already-exists',
544:                         'A user with this email already exists.'
545:                     );
546:                 }
547:                 if (firebaseError.code === 'auth/invalid-email') {
548:                     throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
549:                         'invalid-argument',
550:                         'The email address is invalid.'
551:                     );
552:                 }
553:                 if (firebaseError.code === 'auth/weak-password') {
554:                     throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
555:                         'invalid-argument',
556:                         'The password is too weak.'
557:                     );
558:                 }
559:             }
560: 
561:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
562:                 'internal',
563:                 'Failed to create user account. Please try again.'
564:             );
565:         }
566:     }
567: );
568: 
569: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
570: // FCM Push Notification Functions
571: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
572: 
573: const messaging = admin.messaging();
574: 
575: /**
576:  * Firestore trigger: whenever a new notification document is created,
577:  * look up the target user's FCM token and send a push notification.
578:  *
579:  * Expected document shape (from NotificationModel.toFirestore):
580:  *   userId, title, body, type, data, isRead, createdAt,
581:  *   appointmentId, scheduledFor, reminderType, isDelivered
582:  */
583: export const onNotificationCreated = functions.firestore
584:     .onDocumentCreated('notifications/{notificationId}', async (event) => {
585:         const snap = event.data;
586:         if (!snap) {
587:             console.log('No snapshot in event, skipping.');
588:             return;
589:         }
590:         const notification = snap.data();
591:         const notificationId = event.params.notificationId;
592: 
593:         if (!notification) {
594:             console.log('Empty notification document, skipping.');
595:             return;
596:         }
597: 
598:         const userId: string = notification.userId;
599:         if (!userId) {
600:             console.log('No userId on notification, skipping.');
601:             return;
602:         }
603: 
604:         // If scheduledFor is in the future, skip sending now.
605:         // A scheduled Cloud Task or cron job should handle future delivery.
606:         if (notification.scheduledFor) {
607:             const scheduledTime = notification.scheduledFor.toDate
608:                 ? notification.scheduledFor.toDate()
609:                 : new Date(notification.scheduledFor);
610:             if (scheduledTime > new Date()) {
611:                 console.log(`Notification ${notificationId} is scheduled for the future, skipping immediate send.`);
612:                 return;
613:             }
614:         }
615: 
616:         try {
617:             // Look up the user's FCM token from user_tokens collection
618:             const tokenDoc = await db.collection('user_tokens').doc(userId).get();
619:             const tokenData = tokenDoc.data();
620: 
621:             if (!tokenDoc.exists || !tokenData?.token) {
622:                 console.log(`No FCM token found for user ${userId}, skipping push.`);
623:                 // Still mark as delivered so the in-app notification list shows it
624:                 await snap.ref.update({ isDelivered: true });
625:                 return;
626:             }
627: 
628:             const fcmToken: string = tokenData.token;
629: 
630:             // Build the FCM message
631:             const message: admin.messaging.Message = {
632:                 token: fcmToken,
633:                 notification: {
634:                     title: notification.title || 'UHC Notification',
635:                     body: notification.body || '',
636:                 },
637:                 data: {
638:                     notificationId: notificationId,
639:                     type: notification.type || 'systemUpdate',
640:                     ...(notification.appointmentId && { appointmentId: notification.appointmentId }),
641:                     // Flatten extra data fields for FCM (values must be strings)
642:                     ...(notification.data && Object.fromEntries(
643:                         Object.entries(notification.data).map(([k, v]) => [k, String(v)])
644:                     )),
645:                 },
646:                 android: {
647:                     priority: 'high',
648:                     notification: {
649:                         channelId: 'uhc_notifications',
650:                         priority: 'high',
651:                         sound: 'default',
652:                     },
653:                 },
654:                 apns: {
655:                     payload: {
656:                         aps: {
657:                             alert: {
658:                                 title: notification.title || 'UHC Notification',
659:                                 body: notification.body || '',
660:                             },
661:                             sound: 'default',
662:                             badge: 1,
663:                         },
664:                     },
665:                 },
666:             };
667: 
668:             await messaging.send(message);
669:             console.log(`FCM sent to user ${userId} for notification ${notificationId}`);
670: 
671:             // Mark the notification as delivered in Firestore
672:             await snap.ref.update({ isDelivered: true });
673:         } catch (error: unknown) {
674:             console.error(`Error sending FCM for notification ${notificationId}:`, error);
675: 
676:             // If the token is invalid/expired, clean it up
677:             if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'code' in error) {
678:                 const fcmError = error as { code: string };
679:                 if (
680:                     fcmError.code === 'messaging/invalid-registration-token' ||
681:                     fcmError.code === 'messaging/registration-token-not-registered'
682:                 ) {
683:                     console.log(`Removing stale FCM token for user ${userId}`);
684:                     await db.collection('user_tokens').doc(userId).delete().catch(() => { });
685:                 }
686:             }
687: 
688:             // Still mark as delivered so it shows in the in-app list
689:             await snap.ref.update({ isDelivered: true });
690:         }
691:     });
692: 
693: interface TopicNotificationData {
694:     topic: string;
695:     title: string;
696:     body: string;
697:     data?: Record<string, string>;
698: }
699: 
700: /**
701:  * Callable Cloud Function for admins to send notifications to FCM topics
702:  * (e.g. "announcements", "department_cardiology").
703:  */
704: export const sendTopicNotification = functions.https.onCall(
705:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<TopicNotificationData>) => {
706:         const data = request.data;
707:         const context = request;
708: 
709:         if (!context.auth) {
710:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
711:                 'unauthenticated',
712:                 'You must be logged in to perform this action.'
713:             );
714:         }
715: 
716:         // Verify caller is admin
717:         const callerDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(context.auth.uid).get();
718:         if (!callerDoc.exists || !isAdminOrSuperAdmin(callerDoc.data()?.role)) {
719:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
720:                 'permission-denied',
721:                 'Only admins can send topic notifications.'
722:             );
723:         }
724: 
725:         if (!data.topic || !data.title || !data.body) {
726:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
727:                 'invalid-argument',
728:                 'Missing required fields: topic, title, body'
729:             );
730:         }
731: 
732:         try {
733:             const message: admin.messaging.Message = {
734:                 topic: data.topic,
735:                 notification: {
736:                     title: data.title,
737:                     body: data.body,
738:                 },
739:                 data: data.data || {},
740:                 android: {
741:                     priority: 'high',
742:                     notification: {
743:                         channelId: 'uhc_notifications',
744:                         sound: 'default',
745:                     },
746:                 },
747:                 apns: {
748:                     payload: {
749:                         aps: {
750:                             sound: 'default',
751:                         },
752:                     },
753:                 },
754:             };
755: 
756:             const messageId = await messaging.send(message);
757:             console.log(`Topic notification sent to "${data.topic}", messageId: ${messageId}`);
758: 
759:             return {
760:                 success: true,
761:                 messageId,
762:                 message: `Notification sent to topic "${data.topic}" successfully`,
763:             };
764:         } catch (error) {
765:             console.error('Error sending topic notification:', error);
766:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
767:                 'internal',
768:                 'Failed to send topic notification.'
769:             );
770:         }
771:     }
772: );

774: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
775: // Super Admin Governance Functions
776: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
777: 
778: /**
779:  * Create an admin account. Super Admin only.
780:  */
781: export const createAdminAccount = functions.https.onCall(
782:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
783:         email: string; password: string; fullName: string;
784:         phoneNumber?: string; dateOfBirth?: string; photoUrl?: string;
785:     }>) => {
786:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
787:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
788:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
789:         const data = request.data;
790: 
791:         if (!data.email || !data.password || !data.fullName) {
792:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Missing required fields.');
793:         }
794:         if (data.password.length < 6) {
795:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Password must be at least 6 characters.');
796:         }
797: 
798:         try {
799:             const userRecord = await auth.createUser({
800:                 email: data.email, password: data.password,
801:                 displayName: data.fullName, emailVerified: false,
802:             });
803:             const now = admin.firestore.Timestamp.now();
804:             await db.collection('users').doc(userRecord.uid).set({
805:                 email: data.email, fullName: data.fullName, role: 'admin',
806:                 phoneNumber: data.phoneNumber || null, photoUrl: data.photoUrl || null,
807:                 dateOfBirth: data.dateOfBirth ? admin.firestore.Timestamp.fromDate(new Date(data.dateOfBirth)) : null,
808:                 isActive: true, adminPermissions: null, // full access by default
809:                 notificationSettings: { email: true, push: true, sms: false },
810:                 language: 'en', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
811:                 bloodType: null, allergies: null, studentId: null, staffId: null,
812:             });
813:             await writeAdminAuditLog({
814:                 actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: callerDoc.data()!.role,
815:                 actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
816:                 targetUid: userRecord.uid, targetName: data.fullName,
817:                 targetRoleAfter: 'admin', action: 'admin.create',
818:             });
819:             return { success: true, userId: userRecord.uid, message: 'Admin account created successfully' };
820:         } catch (error: unknown) {
821:             if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'code' in error) {
822:                 const e = error as { code: string };
823:                 if (e.code === 'auth/email-already-exists')
824:                     throw new functions.https.HttpsError('already-exists', 'A user with this email already exists.');
825:             }
826:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('internal', 'Failed to create admin account.');
827:         }
828:     }
829: );
830: 
831: /**
832:  * Change an admin user's role. Super Admin only.
833:  */
834: export const changeAdminRole = functions.https.onCall(
835:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; newRole: string }>) => {
836:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
837:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
838:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
839:         const { targetUid, newRole } = request.data;
840: 
841:         if (!targetUid || !newRole) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Missing targetUid or newRole.');
842:         if (!['admin', 'student', 'staff'].includes(newRole))
843:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Invalid role. Cannot assign doctor or superAdmin via this function.');
844: 
845:         const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
846:         if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
847:         const targetData = targetDoc.data()!;
848:         const oldRole = targetData.role;
849: 
850:         if (oldRole === 'superAdmin')
851:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot change a Super Admin role via this function.');
852: 
853:         await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({ role: newRole, updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now() });
854:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
855:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
856:             targetUid, targetName: targetData.fullName,
857:             targetRoleBefore: oldRole, targetRoleAfter: newRole,
858:             action: oldRole === 'admin' ? 'admin.demote' : 'admin.promote',
859:         });
860:         return { success: true, message: `Role changed from ${oldRole} to ${newRole}` };
861:     }
862: );
863: 
864: /**
865:  * Activate or deactivate an admin. Super Admin only.
866:  */
867: export const setAdminActiveStatus = functions.https.onCall(
868:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; isActive: boolean }>) => {
869:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
870:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
871:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
872:         const { targetUid, isActive } = request.data;
873: 
874:         const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
875:         if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
876:         if (targetDoc.data()!.role === 'superAdmin')
877:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot deactivate a Super Admin via this function.');
878: 
879:         await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({ isActive, updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now() });
880:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
881:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
882:             targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
883:             action: isActive ? 'admin.activate' : 'admin.deactivate',
884:         });
885:         return { success: true, message: isActive ? 'Admin activated' : 'Admin deactivated' };
886:     }
887: );
888: 
889: /**
890:  * Reset an admin's password. Super Admin only.
891:  */
892: export const resetAdminPassword = functions.https.onCall(
893:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; newPassword: string }>) => {
894:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
895:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
896:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
897:         const { targetUid, newPassword } = request.data;
898: 
899:         if (!newPassword || newPassword.length < 6)
900:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Password must be at least 6 characters.');
901:         const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
902:         if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
903: 
904:         await auth.updateUser(targetUid, { password: newPassword });
905:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
906:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
907:             targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
908:             action: 'admin.passwordReset',
909:         });
910:         return { success: true, message: 'Password reset successfully' };
911:     }
912: );

914: /**
915:  * Delete an admin account. Super Admin only.
916:  */
917: export const deleteAdminAccount = functions.https.onCall(
918:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string }>) => {
919:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
920:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
921:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
922:         const { targetUid } = request.data;
923: 
924:         const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
925:         if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
926:         const targetData = targetDoc.data()!;
927:         if (targetData.role === 'superAdmin')
928:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot delete a Super Admin account.');
929: 
930:         try { await auth.deleteUser(targetUid); } catch (e) { console.log('Auth user may not exist:', e); }
931:         await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).delete();
932:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
933:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
934:             targetUid, targetName: targetData.fullName,
935:             targetRoleBefore: targetData.role, action: 'admin.delete',
936:         });
937:         return { success: true, message: 'Admin account deleted successfully' };
938:     }
939: );
940: 
941: /**
942:  * Force sign-out a user by revoking refresh tokens. Super Admin only.
943:  */
944: export const forceSignOutUser = functions.https.onCall(
945:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string }>) => {
946:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
947:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
948:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
949:         const { targetUid } = request.data;
950: 
951:         const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
952:         if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
953: 
954:         await auth.revokeRefreshTokens(targetUid);
955:         // Also remove FCM token to stop push notifications
956:         await db.collection('user_tokens').doc(targetUid).delete().catch(() => {});
957:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
958:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
959:             targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
960:             action: 'admin.forceSignOut',
961:         });
962:         return { success: true, message: 'User sessions revoked' };
963:     }
964: );

966: /**
967:  * Set admin permissions. Super Admin only.
968:  */
969: export const setAdminPermissions = functions.https.onCall(
970:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
971:         targetUid: string;
972:         permissions: Record<string, boolean>;
973:     }>) => {
974:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
975:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
976:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
977:         const { targetUid, permissions } = request.data;
978: 
979:         const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
980:         if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
981:         if (targetDoc.data()!.role !== 'admin')
982:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Permissions can only be set on admin accounts.');
983: 
984:         const oldPerms = targetDoc.data()!.adminPermissions || {};
985:         await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({
986:             adminPermissions: permissions,
987:             updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
988:         });
989:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
990:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
991:             targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
992:             action: 'admin.permissionsUpdate',
993:             before: oldPerms as Record<string, unknown>,
994:             after: permissions as Record<string, unknown>,
995:         });
996:         return { success: true, message: 'Permissions updated' };
997:     }
998: );

1000: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1001: // Super Admin Slot Management (strict two-account model)
1002: // ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1003: 
1004: /**
1005:  * Assign a user to a Super Admin slot (primary or backup).
1006:  * Runs inside a Firestore transaction to enforce constraints:
1007:  * - Max 2 superAdmins total
1008:  * - Exactly one primary, exactly one backup
1009:  * Super Admin only.
1010:  */
1011: export const assignSuperAdminSlot = functions.https.onCall(
1012:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
1013:         targetUid: string; slotType: 'primary' | 'backup';
1014:     }>) => {
1015:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
1016:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
1017:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
1018:         const { targetUid, slotType } = request.data;
1019: 
1020:         if (!['primary', 'backup'].includes(slotType))
1021:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'slotType must be primary or backup.');
1022: 
1023:         const result = await db.runTransaction(async (tx) => {
1024:             // Read current super admins
1025:             const superAdminsSnap = await tx.get(
1026:                 db.collection('users').where('role', '==', 'superAdmin')
1027:             );
1028:             const currentSlots = superAdminsSnap.docs.map(d => ({
1029:                 uid: d.id, slotType: d.data().superAdminType as string,
1030:             }));
1031: 
1032:             // Check if this slot is already occupied by someone else
1033:             const existingSlotHolder = currentSlots.find(s => s.slotType === slotType);
1034:             if (existingSlotHolder && existingSlotHolder.uid !== targetUid) {
1035:                 throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
1036:                     'failed-precondition',
1037:                     `The ${slotType} slot is already occupied. Use rotateSuperAdminSlot to replace.`
1038:                 );
1039:             }
1040: 
1041:             // Check max 2
1042:             const otherSuperAdmins = currentSlots.filter(s => s.uid !== targetUid);
1043:             if (otherSuperAdmins.length >= 2) {
1044:                 throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Maximum 2 Super Admin slots reached.');
1045:             }
1046: 
1047:             // Read target
1048:             const targetRef = db.collection('users').doc(targetUid);
1049:             const targetSnap = await tx.get(targetRef);
1050:             if (!targetSnap.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
1051:             const oldRole = targetSnap.data()!.role;
1052: 
1053:             tx.update(targetRef, {
1054:                 role: 'superAdmin', superAdminType: slotType,
1055:                 updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
1056:             });
1057:             return { oldRole, targetName: targetSnap.data()!.fullName };
1058:         });
1059: 
1060:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
1061:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
1062:             targetUid, targetName: result.targetName,
1063:             targetRoleBefore: result.oldRole, targetRoleAfter: 'superAdmin',
1064:             action: 'superAdmin.slotAssign',
1065:             after: { slotType } as Record<string, unknown>,
1066:         });
1067:         return { success: true, message: `Assigned ${slotType} Super Admin slot` };
1068:     }
1069: );
1070: 
1071: /**
1072:  * Rotate a Super Admin slot: demote the current holder and promote the replacement.
1073:  * Runs inside a transaction to ensure atomicity.
1074:  * Super Admin only.
1075:  */
1076: export const rotateSuperAdminSlot = functions.https.onCall(
1077:     async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
1078:         slotType: 'primary' | 'backup'; replacementUid: string;
1079:     }>) => {
1080:         const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
1081:         const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
1082:         requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
1083:         const { slotType, replacementUid } = request.data;
1084: 
1085:         if (!['primary', 'backup'].includes(slotType))
1086:             throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'slotType must be primary or backup.');
1087: 
1088:         const result = await db.runTransaction(async (tx) => {
1089:             // Find current holder of this slot
1090:             const slotSnap = await tx.get(
1091:                 db.collection('users')
1092:                     .where('role', '==', 'superAdmin')
1093:                     .where('superAdminType', '==', slotType)
1094:             );
1095:             if (slotSnap.empty) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', `No current ${slotType} Super Admin found.`);
1096: 
1097:             const currentHolder = slotSnap.docs[0];
1098:             const currentHolderUid = currentHolder.id;
1099: 
1100:             if (currentHolderUid === replacementUid)
1101:                 throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Replacement is already the slot holder.');
1102: 
1103:             // Read replacement
1104:             const replacementRef = db.collection('users').doc(replacementUid);
1105:             const replacementSnap = await tx.get(replacementRef);
1106:             if (!replacementSnap.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Replacement user not found.');
1107: 
1108:             // Demote current holder to admin
1109:             tx.update(db.collection('users').doc(currentHolderUid), {
1110:                 role: 'admin', superAdminType: admin.firestore.FieldValue.delete(),
1111:                 updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
1112:             });
1113:             // Promote replacement
1114:             tx.update(replacementRef, {
1115:                 role: 'superAdmin', superAdminType: slotType,
1116:                 updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
1117:             });
1118:             return {
1119:                 demotedName: currentHolder.data().fullName,
1120:                 demotedUid: currentHolderUid,
1121:                 promotedName: replacementSnap.data()!.fullName,
1122:                 promotedOldRole: replacementSnap.data()!.role,
1123:             };
1124:         });
1125: 
1126:         // Log both actions
1127:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
1128:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
1129:             targetUid: result.demotedUid, targetName: result.demotedName,
1130:             targetRoleBefore: 'superAdmin', targetRoleAfter: 'admin',
1131:             action: 'superAdmin.slotRotate', metadata: { slotType, direction: 'demote' },
1132:         });
1133:         await writeAdminAuditLog({
1134:             actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
1135:             targetUid: replacementUid, targetName: result.promotedName,
1136:             targetRoleBefore: result.promotedOldRole, targetRoleAfter: 'superAdmin',
1137:             action: 'superAdmin.slotRotate', metadata: { slotType, direction: 'promote' },
1138:         });
1139:         return { success: true, message: `Rotated ${slotType} Super Admin slot` };
1140:     }
1141: );

(End of file - total 1141 lines)
</content>
```

## Assistant (Build · GPT-5.3-Codex · 114.7s)

Phase 1 review result: **Changes required**.

I reviewed `functions/src/index.ts` and validated runtime quality checks.  
Per your request, Flutter checks used Dart MCP:

- `dart-mcp-server_analyze_files`: no errors
- `dart-mcp-server_run_tests`: all tests passed
- Cloud Functions compile check (`cmd /c npm run build` in `functions/`): **failed**

**Blocking findings**
- `functions/src/index.ts:39` and `functions/src/index.ts:54` define `requireAdminOrSuperAdmin` and `requirePermission` but they are unused; with `noUnusedLocals: true` this breaks build/deploy.
- `listAdminAuditLogs` callable is missing (required in your Phase 1 plan for audit visibility).
- Admin governance policy bypass still exists via `createUserAccount`:
  - `functions/src/index.ts:440` includes role `'admin'`
  - `functions/src/index.ts:467` allows caller role admin/superAdmin
  - `functions/src/index.ts:483` explicitly allows creating admin
  - This means an **admin can still create another admin**, which violates the intended Super Admin governance model.
- Super Admin slot integrity is not strictly enforced:
  - `assignSuperAdminSlot` can move an existing super admin from one slot to the other and leave the opposite slot empty (`functions/src/index.ts:1023`, `functions/src/index.ts:1053`)
  - `rotateSuperAdminSlot` allows replacement that may already hold the other slot, also leaving one slot empty (`functions/src/index.ts:1088`, `functions/src/index.ts:1114`)
  - This violates the strict `primary + backup` invariant.
- Governance function scope is too broad in a few places:
  - `setAdminActiveStatus` and `deleteAdminAccount` can target non-admin users (`functions/src/index.ts:867`, `functions/src/index.ts:917`)
  - `resetAdminPassword` has no target-role restriction (`functions/src/index.ts:892`)

**Phase 1 checklist status**
- Shared guards: **partial** (added, but not integrated cleanly due build failure)
- Admin governance callable functions: **partial** (core added, `listAdminAuditLogs` missing)
- Super admin slot management: **partial** (exists, but invariant gaps)
- Existing guards updated for super admin: **partial** (updated, but policy bypass remains)
- Audit log writer/schema: **done**

If Antigravity fixes these blockers, send Phase 1 again and I’ll re-review immediately.

---

## User

Phase 1 again and I’ll re-review immediately.

 const db = admin.firestore();
 const auth = admin.auth();
 
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Shared Guards & Helpers
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

+/** Throws if caller is not authenticated. Returns the uid. */
+function requireAuth(context: { auth?: { uid: string } }): string {
+    if (!context.auth) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
+            'unauthenticated',
+            'You must be logged in to perform this action.'
+        );
+    }
+    return context.auth.uid;
+}
+
+/** Fetches the caller's user document. Throws if not found. */
+async function getCallerUserDoc(uid: string): Promise<FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot> {
+    const doc = await db.collection('users').doc(uid).get();
+    if (!doc.exists) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Caller user document not found.');
+    }
+    return doc;
+}
+
+/** Returns true if user role is admin or superAdmin. */
+function isAdminOrSuperAdmin(role: string | undefined): boolean {
+    return role === 'admin' || role === 'superAdmin';
+}
+
+/** Throws if caller is not admin or superAdmin. */
+function requireAdminOrSuperAdmin(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot): void {
+    const role = callerDoc.data()?.role;
+    if (!isAdminOrSuperAdmin(role)) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only admins can perform this action.');
+    }
+}
+
+/** Throws if caller is not superAdmin. */
+function requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot): void {
+    if (callerDoc.data()?.role !== 'superAdmin') {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only Super Admins can perform this action.');
+    }
+}
+
+/** Throws if caller (admin) lacks the given permission. SuperAdmin bypasses. */
+function requirePermission(callerDoc: FirebaseFirestore.DocumentSnapshot, permissionKey: string): void {
+    const data = callerDoc.data();
+    if (!data) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Caller data missing.');
+    if (data.role === 'superAdmin') return; // bypass
+    if (data.role !== 'admin') {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', 'Only admins can perform this action.');
+    }
+    const perms = data.adminPermissions as Record<string, boolean> | undefined;
+    // Legacy admins without permissions object get full access
+    if (!perms) return;
+    if (!perms[permissionKey]) {
+        throw new functions.https.HttpsError('permission-denied', `Missing permission: ${permissionKey}`);
+    }
+}
+
+/** Writes an entry to admin_audit_logs collection. */
+async function writeAdminAuditLog(params: {
+    actorUid: string;
+    actorRole: string;
+    actorName?: string;
+    targetUid: string;
+    targetName?: string;
+    targetRoleBefore?: string;
+    targetRoleAfter?: string;
+    action: string;
+    before?: Record<string, unknown>;
+    after?: Record<string, unknown>;
+    metadata?: Record<string, unknown>;
+}): Promise<void> {
+    await db.collection('admin_audit_logs').add({
+        ...params,
+        createdAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+    });
+}

+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Super Admin Governance Functions

+/**
+ * Create an admin account. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const createAdminAccount = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        email: string; password: string; fullName: string;
+        phoneNumber?: string; dateOfBirth?: string; photoUrl?: string;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const data = request.data;
+
+        if (!data.email || !data.password || !data.fullName) {
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Missing required fields.');
+        }
+        if (data.password.length < 6) {
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Password must be at least 6 characters.');
+        }
+
+        try {
+            const userRecord = await auth.createUser({
+                email: data.email, password: data.password,
+                displayName: data.fullName, emailVerified: false,
+            });
+            const now = admin.firestore.Timestamp.now();
+            await db.collection('users').doc(userRecord.uid).set({
+                email: data.email, fullName: data.fullName, role: 'admin',
+                phoneNumber: data.phoneNumber || null, photoUrl: data.photoUrl || null,
+                dateOfBirth: data.dateOfBirth ? admin.firestore.Timestamp.fromDate(new Date(data.dateOfBirth)) : null,
+                isActive: true, adminPermissions: null, // full access by default
+                notificationSettings: { email: true, push: true, sms: false },
+                language: 'en', createdAt: now, updatedAt: now,
+                bloodType: null, allergies: null, studentId: null, staffId: null,
+            });
+            await writeAdminAuditLog({
+                actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: callerDoc.data()!.role,
+                actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+                targetUid: userRecord.uid, targetName: data.fullName,
+                targetRoleAfter: 'admin', action: 'admin.create',
+            });
+            return { success: true, userId: userRecord.uid, message: 'Admin account created successfully' };
+        } catch (error: unknown) {
+            if (error && typeof error === 'object' && 'code' in error) {
+                const e = error as { code: string };
+                if (e.code === 'auth/email-already-exists')
+                    throw new functions.https.HttpsError('already-exists', 'A user with this email already exists.');
+            }
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('internal', 'Failed to create admin account.');
+        }
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Change an admin user's role. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const changeAdminRole = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; newRole: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, newRole } = request.data;
+
+        if (!targetUid || !newRole) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Missing targetUid or newRole.');
+        if (!['admin', 'student', 'staff'].includes(newRole))
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Invalid role. Cannot assign doctor or superAdmin via this function.');
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        const targetData = targetDoc.data()!;
+        const oldRole = targetData.role;
+
+        if (oldRole === 'superAdmin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Cannot change a Super Admin role via this function.');
+
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({ role: newRole, updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now() });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetData.fullName,
+            targetRoleBefore: oldRole, targetRoleAfter: newRole,
+            action: oldRole === 'admin' ? 'admin.demote' : 'admin.promote',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: `Role changed from ${oldRole} to ${newRole}` };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Activate or deactivate an admin. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const setAdminActiveStatus = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; isActive: boolean }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, isActive } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        const targetRole = targetDoc.data()!.role;
+        if (targetRole !== 'admin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'This function can only target admin accounts.');
+
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({ isActive, updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now() });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: isActive ? 'admin.activate' : 'admin.deactivate',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: isActive ? 'Admin activated' : 'Admin deactivated' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Reset an admin's password. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const resetAdminPassword = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string; newPassword: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, newPassword } = request.data;
+
+        if (!newPassword || newPassword.length < 6)
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'Password must be at least 6 characters.');
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        if (targetDoc.data()!.role !== 'admin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'This function can only target admin accounts.');
+
+        await auth.updateUser(targetUid, { password: newPassword });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: 'admin.passwordReset',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'Password reset successfully' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Delete an admin account. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const deleteAdminAccount = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        const targetData = targetDoc.data()!;
+        if (targetData.role !== 'admin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'This function can only target admin accounts.');
+
+        try { await auth.deleteUser(targetUid); } catch (e) { console.log('Auth user may not exist:', e); }
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).delete();
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetData.fullName,
+            targetRoleBefore: targetData.role, action: 'admin.delete',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'Admin account deleted successfully' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Force sign-out a user by revoking refresh tokens. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const forceSignOutUser = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{ targetUid: string }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+
+        await auth.revokeRefreshTokens(targetUid);
+        // Also remove FCM token to stop push notifications
+        await db.collection('user_tokens').doc(targetUid).delete().catch(() => {});
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: 'admin.forceSignOut',
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'User sessions revoked' };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Set admin permissions. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const setAdminPermissions = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        targetUid: string;
+        permissions: Record<string, boolean>;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, permissions } = request.data;
+
+        const targetDoc = await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).get();
+        if (!targetDoc.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+        if (targetDoc.data()!.role !== 'admin')
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Permissions can only be set on admin accounts.');
+
+        const oldPerms = targetDoc.data()!.adminPermissions || {};
+        await db.collection('users').doc(targetUid).update({
+            adminPermissions: permissions,
+            updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+        });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: targetDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            action: 'admin.permissionsUpdate',
+            before: oldPerms as Record<string, unknown>,
+            after: permissions as Record<string, unknown>,
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: 'Permissions updated' };
+    }
+);
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Super Admin Slot Management (strict two-account model)
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/**
+ * Assign a user to a Super Admin slot (primary or backup).
+ * Runs inside a Firestore transaction to enforce constraints:
+ * - Max 2 superAdmins total
+ * - Exactly one primary, exactly one backup
+ * Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const assignSuperAdminSlot = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        targetUid: string; slotType: 'primary' | 'backup';
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { targetUid, slotType } = request.data;
+
+        if (!['primary', 'backup'].includes(slotType))
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'slotType must be primary or backup.');
+
+        const result = await db.runTransaction(async (tx) => {
+            // Read current super admins
+            const superAdminsSnap = await tx.get(
+                db.collection('users').where('role', '==', 'superAdmin')
+            );
+            const currentSlots = superAdminsSnap.docs.map(d => ({
+                uid: d.id, slotType: d.data().superAdminType as string,
+            }));
+
+            // Check if this slot is already occupied by someone else
+            const existingSlotHolder = currentSlots.find(s => s.slotType === slotType);
+            if (existingSlotHolder && existingSlotHolder.uid !== targetUid) {
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
+                    'failed-precondition',
+                    `The ${slotType} slot is already occupied. Use rotateSuperAdminSlot to replace.`
+                );
+            }
+
+            // Check max 2
+            const otherSuperAdmins = currentSlots.filter(s => s.uid !== targetUid);
+            if (otherSuperAdmins.length >= 2) {
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Maximum 2 Super Admin slots reached.');
+            }
+
+            // Read target
+            const targetRef = db.collection('users').doc(targetUid);
+            const targetSnap = await tx.get(targetRef);
+            if (!targetSnap.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Target user not found.');
+            const oldRole = targetSnap.data()!.role;
+
+            // Block existing superAdmins from switching slots (would orphan the other slot)
+            if (oldRole === 'superAdmin') {
+                const currentSlotType = targetSnap.data()!.superAdminType;
+                if (currentSlotType && currentSlotType !== slotType) {
+                    throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
+                        'failed-precondition',
+                        `Target already holds the ${currentSlotType} slot. Use rotateSuperAdminSlot to replace.`
+                    );
+                }
+            }
+
+            tx.update(targetRef, {
+                role: 'superAdmin', superAdminType: slotType,
+                updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+            });
+            return { oldRole, targetName: targetSnap.data()!.fullName };
+        });
+
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid, targetName: result.targetName,
+            targetRoleBefore: result.oldRole, targetRoleAfter: 'superAdmin',
+            action: 'superAdmin.slotAssign',
+            after: { slotType } as Record<string, unknown>,
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: `Assigned ${slotType} Super Admin slot` };
+    }
+);
+
+/**
+ * Rotate a Super Admin slot: demote the current holder and promote the replacement.
+ * Runs inside a transaction to ensure atomicity.
+ * Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const rotateSuperAdminSlot = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        slotType: 'primary' | 'backup'; replacementUid: string;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { slotType, replacementUid } = request.data;
+
+        if (!['primary', 'backup'].includes(slotType))
+            throw new functions.https.HttpsError('invalid-argument', 'slotType must be primary or backup.');
+
+        const result = await db.runTransaction(async (tx) => {
+            // Find current holder of this slot
+            const slotSnap = await tx.get(
+                db.collection('users')
+                    .where('role', '==', 'superAdmin')
+                    .where('superAdminType', '==', slotType)
+            );
+            if (slotSnap.empty) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', `No current ${slotType} Super Admin found.`);
+
+            const currentHolder = slotSnap.docs[0];
+            const currentHolderUid = currentHolder.id;
+
+            if (currentHolderUid === replacementUid)
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError('failed-precondition', 'Replacement is already the slot holder.');
+
+            // Read replacement
+            const replacementRef = db.collection('users').doc(replacementUid);
+            const replacementSnap = await tx.get(replacementRef);
+            if (!replacementSnap.exists) throw new functions.https.HttpsError('not-found', 'Replacement user not found.');
+
+            // Block if replacement already holds the OTHER super admin slot
+            if (replacementSnap.data()!.role === 'superAdmin') {
+                throw new functions.https.HttpsError(
+                    'failed-precondition',
+                    'Replacement already holds a Super Admin slot. Demote them first.'
+                );
+            }
+
+            // Demote current holder to admin
+            tx.update(db.collection('users').doc(currentHolderUid), {
+                role: 'admin', superAdminType: admin.firestore.FieldValue.delete(),
+                updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+            });
+            // Promote replacement
+            tx.update(replacementRef, {
+                role: 'superAdmin', superAdminType: slotType,
+                updatedAt: admin.firestore.Timestamp.now(),
+            });
+            return {
+                demotedName: currentHolder.data().fullName,
+                demotedUid: currentHolderUid,
+                promotedName: replacementSnap.data()!.fullName,
+                promotedOldRole: replacementSnap.data()!.role,
+            };
+        });
+
+        // Log both actions
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid: result.demotedUid, targetName: result.demotedName,
+            targetRoleBefore: 'superAdmin', targetRoleAfter: 'admin',
+            action: 'superAdmin.slotRotate', metadata: { slotType, direction: 'demote' },
+        });
+        await writeAdminAuditLog({
+            actorUid: callerUid, actorRole: 'superAdmin', actorName: callerDoc.data()!.fullName,
+            targetUid: replacementUid, targetName: result.promotedName,
+            targetRoleBefore: result.promotedOldRole, targetRoleAfter: 'superAdmin',
+            action: 'superAdmin.slotRotate', metadata: { slotType, direction: 'promote' },
+        });
+        return { success: true, message: `Rotated ${slotType} Super Admin slot` };
+    }
+);
+
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+// Audit Log Query
+// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+/**
+ * List admin audit logs with optional filtering. Super Admin only.
+ */
+export const listAdminAuditLogs = functions.https.onCall(
+    async (request: functions.https.CallableRequest<{
+        limit?: number;
+        targetUid?: string;
+        action?: string;
+    }>) => {
+        const callerUid = requireAuth(request);
+        const callerDoc = await getCallerUserDoc(callerUid);
+        requireSuperAdmin(callerDoc);
+        const { limit: queryLimit, targetUid, action } = request.data || {};
+
+        let query: FirebaseFirestore.Query = db.collection('admin_audit_logs')
+            .orderBy('createdAt', 'desc');
+
+        if (targetUid) query = query.where('targetUid', '==', targetUid);
+        if (action) query = query.where('action', '==', action);
+        query = query.limit(Math.min(queryLimit || 50, 200));
+
+        const snap = await query.get();
+        const logs = snap.docs.map(doc => ({
+            id: doc.id,
+            ...doc.data(),
+            createdAt: doc.data().createdAt?.toDate?.()?.toISOString() || null,
+        }));
+        return { success: true, logs };
+    }
+);

```

**Phase 1 Review**
- Verdict: **Approved with notes**.
- All Phase 1 checklist items are now present in `functions/src/index.ts`:
  - shared guards/helpers (`requireAuth`, `getCallerUserDoc`, `requireSuperAdmin`, permission helper, audit writer) at `functions/src/index.ts:14`
  - governance callables (create/change/activate/reset/delete/force-signout/set-permissions + audit-log listing) from `functions/src/index.ts:755` and `functions/src/index.ts:1146`
  - slot management with transaction-based checks (`assignSuperAdminSlot`, `rotateSuperAdminSlot`) at `functions/src/index.ts:988` and `functions/src/index.ts:1064`
  - legacy admin-only guards updated to allow `superAdmin` (e.g., `updateDoctorEmail`, `deleteDoctorAccount`, `resetDoctorPassword`, `sendTopicNotification`)
- Previous blockers are fixed: TypeScript build passes (`cmd /c npm run build` in `functions/`), `listAdminAuditLogs` exists, `createUserAccount` no longer allows admin creation, and governance target-role checks were tightened.

- Validation run:
  - Dart MCP `analyze_files`: no errors
  - Dart MCP `run_tests`: all tests passed
  - Functions TS compile: passed

- Non-blocking notes for later hardening:
  - `forceSignOutUser` currently accepts any target user (`functions/src/index.ts:921`), not only admin accounts.
  - `changeAdminRole` currently allows non-admin transitions (e.g., student -> staff) (`functions/src/index.ts:808`), while the feature intent is mostly admin promote/demote.

23:   /// Check if user is logged in
24:   bool get isLoggedIn => currentUser != null;
25: 
26:   /// Sign in with email and password
27:   Future<UserCredential> signInWithEmail({
28:     required String email,
29:     required String password,
30:   }) async {
31:     try {
32:       final credential = await _auth.signInWithEmailAndPassword(
33:         email: email,
34:         password: password,
35:       );
36:       return credential;
37:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
38:       throw _handleAuthException(e);
39:     }
40:   }
41: 
42:   /// Register with email and password
43:   Future<UserCredential> registerWithEmail({
44:     required String email,
45:     required String password,
46:     required String fullName,
47:     String? phoneNumber,
48:     DateTime? dateOfBirth,
49:   }) async {
50:     try {
51:       final credential = await _auth.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(
52:         email: email,
53:         password: password,
54:       );
55: 
56:       // Update display name
57:       await credential.user?.updateDisplayName(fullName);
58: 
59:       // Create user document in Firestore
60:       if (credential.user != null) {
61:         await _createUserDocument(
62:           credential.user!,
63:           fullName,
64:           phoneNumber: phoneNumber,
65:           dateOfBirth: dateOfBirth,
66:         );
67:       }
68: 
69:       return credential;
70:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
71:       throw _handleAuthException(e);
72:     }
73:   }
74: 
75:   /// Sign in with Google
76:   Future<UserCredential?> signInWithGoogle() async {
77:     try {
78:       UserCredential? userCredential;
79: 
80:       if (kIsWeb) {
81:         // On web, use Firebase Auth popup directly
82:         final provider = GoogleAuthProvider();
83:         userCredential = await _auth.signInWithPopup(provider);
84:       } else {
85:         // On mobile, use google_sign_in package
86:         final GoogleSignInAccount? googleUser = await _googleSignIn.signIn();
87: 
88:         if (googleUser == null) {
89:           return null; // User cancelled the sign-in
90:         }
91: 
92:         final GoogleSignInAuthentication googleAuth =
93:             await googleUser.authentication;
94: 
95:         final credential = GoogleAuthProvider.credential(
96:           accessToken: googleAuth.accessToken,
97:           idToken: googleAuth.idToken,
98:         );
99: 
100:         userCredential = await _auth.signInWithCredential(credential);
101:       }
102: 
103:       final user = userCredential.user!;
104: 
105:       // Check if this user already has an account in Firestore
106:       // (created by admin or via email/password registration).
107:       // Google sign-in must NOT create new accounts.
108:       final docRef = _firestore.collection('users').doc(user.uid);
109:       final doc = await docRef.get();
110: 
111:       if (!doc.exists) {
112:         // No account exists — reject this sign-in.
113:         // Delete the Firebase Auth user that was just created and sign out.
114:         await user.delete();
115:         try {
116:           await _googleSignIn.signOut();
117:         } catch (_) {}
118:         throw Exception(
119:           'No account found. Please contact your administrator to create an account.',
120:         );
121:       }
122: 
123:       // Account exists — update last login, preserving existing photo.
124:       await _updateExistingUserDocument(doc, user);
125: 
126:       return userCredential;
127:     } catch (e) {
128:       // Re-throw our custom "no account" error as-is
129:       if (e.toString().contains('No account found')) {
130:         rethrow;
131:       }
132:       throw Exception('Google sign-in failed: $e');
133:     }
134:   }
135: 
136:   /// Check if current user has Google provider linked
137:   bool get isGoogleLinked {
138:     final user = currentUser;
139:     if (user == null) return false;
140:     return user.providerData.any((info) => info.providerId == 'google.com');
141:   }
142: 
143:   /// Get the linked Google email from Firebase Auth provider data
144:   String? get googleEmail {
145:     final user = currentUser;
146:     if (user == null) return null;
147:     try {
148:       final googleInfo = user.providerData.firstWhere(
149:         (info) => info.providerId == 'google.com',
150:       );
151:       return googleInfo.email;
152:     } catch (_) {
153:       return null;
154:     }
155:   }
156: 
157:   /// Link current user's account with Google
158:   Future<UserCredential> linkWithGoogle() async {
159:     final user = currentUser;
160:     if (user == null) {
161:       throw Exception('No user logged in');
162:     }
163: 
164:     try {
165:       if (kIsWeb) {
166:         // On web, use Firebase Auth popup for linking
167:         final provider = GoogleAuthProvider();
168:         final userCredential = await user.linkWithPopup(provider);
169: 
170:         // Save Google email to Firestore
171:         if (userCredential.user != null) {
172:           final googleInfo = userCredential.user!.providerData.firstWhere(
173:             (info) => info.providerId == 'google.com',
174:             orElse: () => userCredential.user!.providerData.first,
175:           );
176:           await _firestore.collection('users').doc(user.uid).update({
177:             'updatedAt': Timestamp.fromDate(DateTime.now()),
178:             'googleEmail': googleInfo.email,
179:           });
180:         }
181:         return userCredential;
182:       }
183: 
184:       // On mobile, use google_sign_in package
185:       final GoogleSignInAccount? googleUser = await _googleSignIn.signIn();
186:       if (googleUser == null) {
187:         throw Exception('Google sign-in cancelled');
188:       }
189: 
190:       final GoogleSignInAuthentication googleAuth =
191:           await googleUser.authentication;
192: 
193:       final credential = GoogleAuthProvider.credential(
194:         accessToken: googleAuth.accessToken,
195:         idToken: googleAuth.idToken,
196:       );
197: 
198:       final userCredential = await user.linkWithCredential(credential);
199: 
200:       if (userCredential.user != null) {
201:         final googleInfo = userCredential.user!.providerData.firstWhere(
202:           (info) => info.providerId == 'google.com',
203:           orElse: () => userCredential.user!.providerData.first,
204:         );
205:         await _firestore.collection('users').doc(user.uid).update({
206:           'updatedAt': Timestamp.fromDate(DateTime.now()),
207:           'googleEmail': googleInfo.email,
208:         });
209:       }
210: 
211:       return userCredential;
212:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
213:       if (e.code == 'credential-already-in-use') {
214:         throw Exception(
215:             'This Google account is already linked to another user.');
216:       } else if (e.code == 'provider-already-linked') {
217:         throw Exception('A Google account is already linked.');
218:       }
219:       throw _handleAuthException(e);
220:     } catch (e) {
221:       throw Exception('Failed to link Google account: $e');
222:     }
223:   }
224: 
225:   /// Send password reset email
226:   Future<void> sendPasswordResetEmail(String email) async {
227:     try {
228:       await _auth.sendPasswordResetEmail(email: email);
229:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
230:       throw _handleAuthException(e);
231:     }
232:   }
233: 
234:   /// Change user password
235:   Future<void> changePassword(
236:     String currentPassword,
237:     String newPassword,
238:   ) async {
239:     final user = currentUser;
240:     if (user == null || user.email == null) {
241:       throw Exception('No user logged in or user has no email');
242:     }
243: 
244:     try {
245:       // Create credential with current password
246:       final credential = EmailAuthProvider.credential(
247:         email: user.email!,
248:         password: currentPassword,
249:       );
250: 
251:       // Re-authenticate
252:       await user.reauthenticateWithCredential(credential);
253: 
254:       // Update password
255:       await user.updatePassword(newPassword);
256:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
257:       throw _handleAuthException(e);
258:     }
259:   }
260: 
261:   /// Sign out
262:   Future<void> signOut() async {
263:     try {
264:       await _googleSignIn.signOut();
265:     } catch (e) {
266:       // Ignore google sign out errors (common on web if not signed in via google)
267:     }
268:     // Always sign out of Firebase Auth
269:     await _auth.signOut();
270:   }
271: 
272:   /// Create user document in Firestore
273:   Future<void> _createUserDocument(
274:     User user,
275:     String fullName, {
276:     String? phoneNumber,
277:     DateTime? dateOfBirth,
278:   }) async {
279:     final userModel = UserModel(
280:       id: user.uid,
281:       email: user.email ?? '',
282:       fullName: fullName,
283:       photoUrl: user.photoURL,
284:       phoneNumber: phoneNumber,
285:       dateOfBirth: dateOfBirth,
286:       role: UserRole.student,
287:       createdAt: DateTime.now(),
288:       updatedAt: DateTime.now(),
289:     );
290: 
291:     await _firestore
292:         .collection('users')
293:         .doc(user.uid)
294:         .set(userModel.toFirestore());
295:   }
296: 
297:   /// Update existing user document on Google sign-in.
298:   /// Only updates the login timestamp; preserves existing photo.
299:   Future<void> _updateExistingUserDocument(
300:     DocumentSnapshot doc,
301:     User user,
302:   ) async {
303:     final existingData = doc.data() as Map<String, dynamic>?;
304:     final existingPhoto = existingData?['photoUrl'] as String?;
305: 
306:     final updates = <String, dynamic>{
307:       'updatedAt': Timestamp.fromDate(DateTime.now()),
308:     };
309: 
310:     // Only set photoUrl from Google if the user has no existing photo
311:     if ((existingPhoto == null || existingPhoto.isEmpty) &&
312:         user.photoURL != null) {
313:       updates['photoUrl'] = user.photoURL;
314:     }
315: 
316:     await _firestore.collection('users').doc(user.uid).update(updates);
317:   }
318: 
319:   /// Get user data from Firestore
320:   Future<UserModel?> getUserData(String uid) async {
321:     final doc = await _firestore.collection('users').doc(uid).get();
322:     if (doc.exists) {
323:       return UserModel.fromFirestore(doc);
324:     }
325:     return null;
326:   }
327: 
328:   /// Update user profile
329:   Future<void> updateUserProfile({
330:     required String uid,
331:     String? fullName,
332:     String? phoneNumber,
333:     String? photoUrl,
334:     DateTime? dateOfBirth,
335:     String? bloodType,
336:     String? allergies,
337:   }) async {
338:     final updates = <String, dynamic>{
339:       'updatedAt': Timestamp.fromDate(DateTime.now()),
340:     };
341: 
342:     if (fullName != null) updates['fullName'] = fullName;
343:     if (phoneNumber != null) updates['phoneNumber'] = phoneNumber;
344:     if (photoUrl != null) updates['photoUrl'] = photoUrl;
345:     if (dateOfBirth != null) {
346:       updates['dateOfBirth'] = Timestamp.fromDate(dateOfBirth);
347:     }
348:     if (bloodType != null) updates['bloodType'] = bloodType;
349:     if (allergies != null) updates['allergies'] = allergies;
350: 
351:     await _firestore.collection('users').doc(uid).update(updates);
352: 
353:     // Update Firebase Auth display name if changed
354:     if (fullName != null && currentUser != null) {
355:       await currentUser!.updateDisplayName(fullName);
356:     }
357:   }
358: 
359:   /// Upload profile image to Firebase Storage
360:   Future<String> uploadProfileImage(String uid, XFile imageFile) async {
361:     try {
362:       final ref = _storage.ref().child('profile_images').child('$uid.jpg');
363: 
364:       // Use putData for cross-platform compatibility (works on Web & Mobile)
365:       final metadata = SettableMetadata(contentType: 'image/jpeg');
366:       final data = await imageFile.readAsBytes();
367: 
368:       await ref.putData(data, metadata);
369:       final downloadUrl = await ref.getDownloadURL();
370:       return downloadUrl;
371:     } catch (e) {
372:       throw Exception('Failed to upload image: $e');
373:     }
374:   }
375: 
376:   /// Upload profile image from bytes (for Web/Optimized flows)
377:   Future<String> uploadProfileImageBytes(
378:     String uid,
379:     Uint8List data,
380:     String fileName,
381:   ) async {
382:     try {
383:       // Determine content type based on extension or default to jpeg
384:       final extension = fileName.split('.').last.toLowerCase();
385:       String contentType = 'image/jpeg';
386:       if (extension == 'png') contentType = 'image/png';
387:       if (extension == 'webp') contentType = 'image/webp';
388: 
389:       final ref = _storage
390:           .ref()
391:           .child('profile_images')
392:           .child('$uid.${extension == 'jpg' ? 'jpg' : extension}');
393: 
394:       final metadata = SettableMetadata(contentType: contentType);
395: 
396:       await ref.putData(data, metadata);
397:       final downloadUrl = await ref.getDownloadURL();
398:       return downloadUrl;
399:     } catch (e) {
400:       throw Exception('Failed to upload image bytes: $e');
401:     }
402:   }
403: 
404:   /// Update user notification settings
405:   Future<void> updateNotificationSettings(
406:     String uid,
407:     Map<String, dynamic> settings,
408:   ) async {
409:     await _firestore.collection('users').doc(uid).update({
410:       'notificationSettings': settings,
411:       'updatedAt': Timestamp.fromDate(DateTime.now()),
412:     });
413:   }
414: 
415:   /// Handle Firebase Auth exceptions
416:   String _handleAuthException(FirebaseAuthException e) {
417:     switch (e.code) {
418:       case 'user-not-found':
419:         return 'No user found with this email.';
420:       case 'wrong-password':
421:         return 'Incorrect password.';
422:       case 'email-already-in-use':
423:         return 'This email is already registered.';
424:       case 'weak-password':
425:         return 'Password is too weak.';
426:       case 'invalid-email':
427:         return 'Invalid email address.';
428:       case 'user-disabled':
429:         return 'This account has been disabled.';
430:       case 'too-many-requests':
431:         return 'Too many attempts. Please try again later.';
432:       default:
433:         return e.message ?? 'An error occurred.';
434:     }
435:   }
436: }
